---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** tatra sarvāsām
evaika-jātīya-bhāvatvāt kurary-ādi-vāk-śravaṇena vakṣyamāṇā vāco jātā
ity āha---**śrī-mahiṣya ūcur** iti \| tatra svabhāvata eva ruvatīṁ
kurarīṁ praty āhuḥ---he **kurari** ! **jagati tvam** evaikā satī **na
śeṣe** śayanecchām api na kuruṣa ity arthaḥ \| yato **vilapasi** uccaiḥ
paridevanām eva kuruṣe \| **īśvaro**'smākaṁ patis tu **rātryāṁ**
tad-anveṣaṇa-śakti-virodhinyāṁ **gupta-bodhaḥ** kutrāpy ācchannaḥ san
śete \|

yad vā, **jagati** ity asyaivātraivānvayaḥ \| kutrāpīty evārthaḥ \|
tasmād idam anumīmaha ity āhuḥ---**vayam iva** iti \| tasmāt he
**sakhi** ! sādṛśyāt sakhyaṁ prāpteḥ yuktam eva mamedam iti tavoccair
vilāpo'yam asmāsv api sācivyāya syād iti bhāvaḥ \|\|15\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** tad evāha---**kurari**
ity-ādi \| sarva-bhūteṣu yaḥ paśyed bhagavad-bhāvam ātmanaḥ \[bhā.pu.
11.2.45\] ity-ādi-diśā ātmano bhagavati yo bhāvaḥ, taṁ sarva-bhūteṣu
paśyantīnāṁ, praṇaya-raśanayā dhṛtāṅghri-padmaḥ \[bhā.pu. 11.2.55\]
ity-ādinā vivriyamāṇam uttama-bhāgavata-daśām ārūḍhānāṁ mahiṣīṇāṁ pṛthak
pṛthag bhāsamānam idam---he **kurari** ! **īśvaraḥ** śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ
**svapiti**, **tvaṁ vilapasi**, keyaṁ te rītiḥ ? tan-nidrā-bhaṅge bhayaṁ
na karoṣi ?

nanu svapan katham asau mad-vilāpaṁ śroṣyati ? ity
āha---**agupta-bodhaḥ** \| nidrāyām apy aguptaḥ prakaṭo bodho yasya,
ataḥ śroṣyaty eva, tato mā vilapeti śeṣaḥ \|

athavā, kim iti tvam ākṣipyase ? he **sakhi** ! **vayam iva kaccit
tvam** apy evaṁ, kiṁ tad-vīta-nidrā-kṛt ? jñātam ity āha---**na śeṣe**
na svapiṣi \| tasya kāraṇam āha---**nalina-nayana-** ity-ādi \|
**vayaṁ** yathā tasya **hāsodāra-līlekṣitena nirviṇṇa-cittāḥ** satyo
**vīta-nidrā** bhūtvā na śayāmahe, tathā tvam apīti \|\|15\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (prīti-sandarbhaḥ 387) :** atha viraha-sparśīni tāny
evonmāda-vākyāny āhuḥ---**kurari** ity-ādi \| he **kurari** ! **jagati
tvam** eva ekā **rātryāṁ vilapasi,** ata eva **na śeṣe** na nidrāsi \|
**īśvaro**'smat-svāmī tu **gupta-bodhaḥ** kvacid ācchannaḥ svapiti \|
tasmād asmākaṁ tava ca vilāpādi-sādharmyād idam anumīyata ity
āhuḥ---**vayam iva** iti \| evam anyatrāpi yojanīyam \|\|15\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tataś ca ātmano bhāvam
unmāda-vaśāt prāyaḥ sarvatra paśyantyaḥ kurary-ādīn āhur daśabhiḥ \| he
**kurari** ! yasya viraheṇa **tvaṁ vilapasi** **vīta-nidrā** gata-nidrā
satī, sa tu tvayi prema-śūnyaḥ **īśvaro**'smākaṁ patiḥ **svapiti**, atas
tvad-vilāpaṁ na śṛṇoti \| tata eva tvad-vilāpa-śravaṇotthā kṛpāpy asya
sambhavet na yatas tvat-saṅgaṁ kuryāt, kiṁ yuṣmābhiḥ saha **svapiti** ?
nahi nahi, **gupta-bodhaḥ** asmābhir ajñāta-tattva eva **jagaty** asmin
kvāpi **rātryāṁ** tad-anveṣaṇa-virodhinyāṁ **śete** \| atas tvaṁ vā kiṁ
kariṣyasi ? vayaṁ vā kiṁ kurmaḥ ? iti bhāvaḥ \| śiva śiva tvaṁ
pakṣi-jātir api he **sakhi** ! **vayam iva gāḍha-nirviddha-cetā** abhūḥ
! avaśyam evam etat-saṅgo bhavatu iti \| nirbandhe hetuḥ---**nalina-**
ity-ādi \|\|15\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.16 \|\|**

**netre nimīlayasi naktam adṛṣṭa-bandhus**

**tvaṁ roravīṣi karuṇaṁ bata cakravāki \|**

**dāsyaṁ gatā vayam ivācyuta-pāda-juṣṭāṁ**

**kiṁ vā srajaṁ spṛhayase kavareṇa voḍhum \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : naktaṁ** rātrāv **adṛṣṭa-bandhuḥ**
satī **roravīṣi** \| **kiṁ vā** naitavad, api tu **vayam iva spṛhayase**
\|\|16\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** *etāvat*
bandhu-viyoga-mātram eva **spṛhayase** icchasi \| **kavareṇa**
keśa-vinyāsena \|\|16\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**kaivalya-dīpikā :** **netra** iti \| **naktaṁ** rātrau \| **bandhuḥ**
priyatamaḥ \| **roravīṣi** bhṛśaṁ śabdaṁ karoṣi \| **bata** iti khede \|
**acyutasya pādābhyāṁ** bhakty-arpitatvāj **juṣṭāṁ** **vayam iva** yathā
vayaṁ **spṛhayāmaḥ** \| anena saṅkalpa-lakṣaṇā \|\|16\|\| \[mu.pha.
12.73\]

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** bhavatu, tvam eva
pralapa, cakravākī kathaṁ roravītīti tām ākṣipyāhuḥ---**netre** ity-ādi
\| he **cakravāki** ! **tvaṁ** kathaṁ **roravīṣi**, ārta-nādaṁ punaḥ
punaḥ kuruṣe ? tathāpi īśvara-nidrā-bhaṅge bhayaṁ nāste ! āṁ jñātaṁ,
**vayaṁ** yathā, tathā **tvam** apy **acyuta-pāda-juṣṭāṁ srajaṁ voḍhuṁ
spṛhayase**, ata eva **netre nimīlayasi** dhyāyasi dhyānāntaraṁ
**roravīṣi** \| rātrau cakravākādarśanenāhaṁ roravīmi ? tatrāha---**na,
adṛṣṭa-bandhuḥ**, dṛṣṭa-bandhur eva tvam \| asyām upari kasyāpi
kāla-kṛta-doṣo nāsti, īśvara-prasādāt \| tathāpi ced evaṁ tavānumitam
idaṁ **vayam iva** iti \|\|16\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** tasyā apy adhikam
ārta-nādaṁ cakravākyāḥ śrutvā tathaivāhuḥ---**netre** iti \| **bandhuḥ**
priyatamaḥ **karuṇaṁ** yathā syāt, tathā **roravīṣi**, bhṛśam ārta-nādaṁ
tanoṣi \| **bata** khede \| aho bata īdṛśa ārta-nādaḥ
sva-paty-adarśana-mātreṇa na syāt, kintu śrī-bhagavati
bhāva-viśeṣeṇaiveti pakṣāntaram āhuḥ---**dāsyam** iti \|
tad-ekādhīnatvaṁ prāptā **vayam iva** yathā vayaṁ spṛhayāmaḥ \| yad vā,
**vayam iva dāsyaṁ** dāsī-matitvaṁ **gatā** **acyutasya** sadā
sarva-sad-guṇa-rūpādi-paripūrṇasya bhagavataḥ **pādābhyāṁ juṣṭām** sadā
prītyā svīkṛtāṁ **voḍhuṁ spṛhayase** spṛhayasi \| idaṁ
dāsya-prāpti-prayojanam \| tathā coktaṁ śrī-yajña-patnībhiḥ---prāptā
vayaṁ tulasi-dāma padāvasṛṣṭaṁ keśair nivoḍhum \[bhā.pu. 10.23.29\][^3]
iti \| karaṇena keśa-pāśeneti tasyās tad-abhāve'pi tad-uktir ātmoddeśāt
premonmādād eva vā \| tad uktam eva---**unmattavad** iti \| evam agre'pi
\| anyat tair vyākhyātam \|

yad vā, **kiṁ vā** iti \| **kiṁ** tarke \| bhāva-viśeṣeṇa
srag-vahana-spṛhayaiva roravīṣīti tarkayāma ity arthaḥ \|\|16\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** tasyā apy adhikam ārta-nādaṁ
cakravākyāḥ śrutvā tathaivāhuḥ---**netre** iti \| **bandhuḥ** priyatamaḥ
\| **karuṇaṁ** yathā syāt, tathā **roravīṣi**, bhṛśam ārta-nādaṁ tanoṣi
\| **bata** khede \| asmat-samaiva tvam apīti bhāvaḥ \| aho **bata**
īdṛśa ārta-nādaḥ sva-paty-adarśana-mātreṇa na syāt, kintu śrī-bhagavati
bhāva-viśeṣeṇaiveti pakṣāntaram āhuḥ---**dāsyam** iti \| **vayam iva
dāsyaṁ gatā** dāsī satī **acyutasya** sadā
sarva-guṇa-rūpādi-paripūrṇasya bhagavataḥ **pādābhyāṁ juṣṭām**
upabhuktāṁ caraṇopadhānī-kṛtāṁ **voḍhuṁ spṛhayase** spṛhayasi \|
bhāva-viśeṣeṇa paramparayā tac-caraṇa-sparśaṁ kāmayasa ity arthaḥ \|
**pāda**-śabdo'tra pātivratyocita-bhaktyā śrī-bhagavat-spṛṣṭatā-mātre tu
tātparyam \|

yad vā, **vayam iva dāsyaṁ gatā** asīti tāṁ tathā **voḍhuṁ spṛhayasi**
iti kāntā bhūtvā tad-ucita-saubhāgyam icchasīty arthaḥ \|
spaṣṭatayānuktis tu śālīnyāt \| yathoktaṁ yajña-patnībhiḥ---prāptā vayaṁ
tulasi-dāma padāvasṛṣṭaṁ \[bhā.pu. 10.23.29\][^4] iti \|\|16\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** pratyuvāca---he sakhi !
kurary eva pralapatu, katham iyaṁ cakravākī rauti ? ity āha---**netra**
ity-ādi \| he **cakravāki** ! kim iti **roravīṣi** ?
tavāpīśvara-nidrā-bhaṅga-bhayaṁ nāsti \| ajñātaṁ **vayam iva dāsyaṁ
gatā** satī **acyuta-pāda-juṣṭāṁ srajaṁ kavareṇa voḍhuṁ spṛhayase,** tad
yuktam evedaṁ te samākrandanam \| ata eva **netre nimīlayasi** dhyāyasi
\| \"na tv ahaṁ cakravākādarśanena roravīmi,
tavāpīśvara-nidrā-bhaṅga-bhayaṁ na tad\" ity atrāśaṅkasa ity āha---na,
**adṛṣṭa-bandhur** eva bhavati \| asyāṁ puri kasyāpy abhīṣṭa-vicchedo
nāsti, īśvarasya prabhāvāt \| tathāpi yad eva **roravīṣi**, tena yad
anumitaṁ, tad eva satyam iti bhāvaḥ \|\|16\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : adṛṣṭa-bandhuḥ** kim
adṛṣṭa-sva-bhartṛkāsi ? aho **bata** īdṛśa ārta-nādaḥ
sva-paty-adarśanena sambhaved iti pakṣāntaram āhuḥ---**dāsyaṁ gatā** iti
\|\|15\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.17 \|\|**

**bho bhoḥ sadā niṣṭanase udanvann**

**alabdha-nidro'dhigata-prajāgaraḥ \|**

**kiṁ vā mukundāpahṛtātma-lāñchanaḥ**

**prāptāṁ daśāṁ tvaṁ ca gato duratyayām \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : alabdha-nidraḥ sadā niṣṭanase**
krośasi \| kiṁ vā, asmābhiḥ **prāptāṁ daśāṁ** **tvam** api **gato**'si
\| aho kaṣṭaṁ ! yathā vayaṁ sambhogena
**mukundāpahṛta**-kuca-kuṅkumādi-**lāñchanāḥ,** tathā tvam api,
yato'pahṛta-śrī-kaustubhādi-lāñchano lakṣyase \|\|17\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** **niṣṭanase** ṣṭan-śabde
ni-pūrvaḥ \| **duratyayāṁ** durlaṅghyām \|\|17\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**kaivalya-dīpikā :** **bho** iti \| **he udanvan** samudra !
**niṣṭanase** nitarāṁ śabdāyase \| **mukundāpahṛtam** ākṛṣṭaṁ yad
**ātmano** **lāñchanaṁ** samudra-śāyanā mūrtiḥ, **tena prāptāṁ daśāṁ
gataḥ** \| **tvaṁ ca** iti ca-kāreṇa vayaṁ ca \| samudra-śāyina eva
puruṣasya kṛṣṇatvāt prati samudraṁ hariḥ śeta iti kavi-samayāc ca \|
atra **niṣṭanasa** ity anena pralāpa-lakṣaṇā \|\|17\|\| \[mu.pha.
12.74\]

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** tādṛśīnāṁ strītvāt
dhairyābhāve samucitam evaitat \| ayaṁ tv atigambhīro'pi samudra
uccaistarām ākrośati kim ? ity āhuḥ---**bho bho** ! ity-ādi \| he
**udanvan** ! samudra ! **sadā** sadaiva **niṣṭanase**,
īśvara-nidrā-bhaṅga-bhayaṁ na karoṣi \| kim idam ? svayam
**alabdha-nidra** īśvarasyāpi nidrā-bhaṅgaṁ karoṣi \| āṁ jñātam \| kiṁ
vā, **mukundāpahṛtātma-lāñchanaḥ** san **duratyayāṁ daśāṁ** **tvaṁ ca**
**prāptaḥ** \| vayaṁ tu duratyayāṁ daśāṁ prāptā eva, tvaṁ ceti \|
ca-kārasyākṣepaḥ \| **mukundenāpahṛto** ya **ātmā,** sa eva
**lāñchanam** udvega-vyañjakaṁ yasya \|\|17\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī** **(bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** tasyā apy adhikataram
ākrośantaṁ samudraṁ tathaivāhuḥ---**bho** iti \|
śrī-bhagavan-mahā-vibhūtitvena sādara-sambodhanam \| vīpsā atikhedāt \|
**alabdha-nidratvād** eva **adhigato**'dhikaṁ prāptaḥ **prakṛṣṭo
jāgaro** yena, tathā-bhūtaḥ san **niṣṭanase** \| **mukundena**
sarvānanda-pradenāpi bhagavatā **hṛtātma-lāñchano** **daśāṁ**
tad-aprāpti-duravasthām \| **ca** api \| tām api **duratyayām**
anatikramyām \| anyat tair vyākhyātam \|

yad vā, **mukundena** iti smitādinā kunda-sundara-śrī-dantāli-prakāśena
śrī-mukha-śobhayeti bhāvaḥ \| **apahṛtam ātma-lāñchanaṁ**
tvat-svābhāvika-sthairya-gāmbhīryādi-lakṣaṇaṁ yasya, tathā-bhūtaḥ san
asmābhiḥ **prāptāṁ** dhairyādi-rahitāṁ **daśāṁ** **tvam** api
**gato**'si, yataḥ **sadā niṣṭanase** \|\|17\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** tasyā apy adhikataram
ākrośantaṁ samudraṁ tathaivāhuḥ---**bho** iti
śrī-bhagavan-mahā-vibhūtitvena sādara-sambodhanam \| vīpsā atikhedāt \|
**alabdha-nidratvād** eva **adhigataḥ** adhikaṁ prāptaḥ **prakṛṣṭo
jāgaro** yena, tathā-bhūtaḥ san kiṁ **niṣṭanase**, asmākaṁ kenāpi
duḥkhena bhavatu nāma, tat tad bhavatu, tad vināpi katham iti bhāvaḥ \|
kṣaṇaṁ vimṛśyāhuḥ---**kiṁ vā** iti \| **mukundena**
sarva-duḥkha-vimocakenāpi **apahṛtam** **ātma-lāñchanaṁ**
svabhāva-siddha-sthairya-gāmbhīryādi-rūpa-lakṣaṇaṁ yasya, tathā-bhūtaḥ
san **tvaṁ ca** asmad-vidhavattvam api **duratyayām** anatikramyāṁ
**daśāṁ** tad-aprāpti-duḥkha-sthāṁ **gato**'si \| hā kaṣṭam iti bhāvaḥ
\|\|17\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** tvādṛśīnāṁ strītvād
dhairyābhāve samucitam evaitat kathanam \| ayaṁ tūccair gabhīro'pi
samudraḥ kathaṁ stanati ? iti kācid aparāha---**bho bho** ity-ādi \| he
**udanvan** ! jaladhe ! **sadaiva niṣṭanase** īśvara-nidrā-bhaṅga-bhayaṁ
kiṁ kuruṣe ? svayam **alabdha-nidrāṁ** ca na yāsi \| āṁ jñātam \| kiṁ
vā, **mukundāpahṛtātma-lāñchanaḥ** sannidhi-gata-prajāgaro **duratyayāṁ
daśāṁ gataḥ** prāptā svayam evotpannā \| **mukundenāpahṛto** ya
**ātmā,** sa eva **lāñchanam** udvega-cihnaṁ yasya, tad ucitam evaitad
iti śeṣaḥ \|\|17\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : bho udanvan** ! gāmbhīryaṁ
parityajya atitarala-loka iti **niṣṭanase** śabdāyase, nirnidraḥ sann
uccaiḥ phūtkṛtya rodiṣi \| atra kāraṇaṁ vada \| athavā, alaṁ
kāraṇa-kathanena \| jñātam asmābhir ity āhuḥ---**kiṁ vā** iti \| yathā
sambhoga-miṣeṇa apahṛtā asmat-kuṅkuma-hāra-mālā kaḥ sa coraḥ, tathaiva
tvam api tenaiva **apahṛta**-śrī-kaustubhādi-**lāñchanaḥ** \|\|16\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.18 \|\|**

**tvaṁ yakṣmaṇā balavatāsi gṛhīta indo**

**kṣīṇas tamo na nija-dīdhitibhiḥ kṣiṇoṣi \|**

**kaccin mukunda-gaditāni yathā vayaṁ tvaṁ**

**vismṛtya bhoḥ sthagita-gīr upalakṣyase naḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : mukunda-gaditāni** rahasyāni
**vismṛtya** tad-eka-cintayā **kaccit tvaṁ** **kṣīṇo'si vayam iva** \|
**sthagita-gīs** tanu-vāk \| he **indo** ! **nas** tathaiva
**upalakṣyase** \|\|18\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** **yakṣmaṇā** kṣaya-rogeṇa,
yakṣmā tu kṣaya-roge syād grahe ca bāla-vṛddhayoḥ iti nāma-mālā \|
**dīdhitiḥ** ghṛṇiḥ \| *tad-eka-cintayā* mukundaika-cintayā \|
**sthagitā** ācchāditā **gīr** yasya, sa tathā \| sthage ācchādane,
tataḥ kte sthagiteti siddheḥ \| **no**'smābhiḥ \| *tathaiva* asmat-tulya
eva \|\|18\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**kaivalya-dīpikā :** **tvam** iti \| **yakṣmaṇā** dakṣa-śāpajena rogeṇa
**prakṣiṇoṣi**, na nāśayasi \| yathā vayaṁ virahajena yakṣmaṇā
**kṣīṇāḥ** \| **tamo**'jñānam \| **dīdhitibhiḥ** prajñā-raśmibhir na
kṣiṇumaḥ \| **viśrutya** viśeṣāt vā **sthagita-gīr** niścalaḥ \|
**upalakṣyase** dṛśyase no'smābhiḥ \| anena vyādhi-lakṣaṇā \|\|18\|\|
\[mu.pha. 12.75\]

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** indum uddiśya kāścid
āhuḥ---**tvaṁ yakṣmaṇā** ity-ādi \| he **indo** ! **kṣīṇaḥ** san
**nija-dīdhitibhis tamo na kṣiṇoṣi** \| ko hetuḥ ? tatrāhuḥ---**kaccid**
ity-ādi \| **yathā vayaṁ**, tathā **tvam** api **sthagita-gīr
upalakṣyase no** asmābhiḥ \| yato **balavatā** **yakṣmaṇā gṛhītaḥ** \|
cintāyāṁ kṣaya-vyādhir bhavati, sā pūrva-rāgasya daśā-daśakāntarvartinī
vyādhi-nāmnī daśā \| tatra hetuḥ---**mukunda-gaditāni** **vismṛtya**
viśeṣeṇa smṛtvā rahasi gaditaṁ tad vismṛtyeti vā, ānandena prāg vismṛtaṁ
paścāt tad-anutāpo jāta iti svānubhava-prakaṭanam \|\|18\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** adhunā mahā-rogārtam iva
candram dṛṣṭvāhuḥ---**tvam** iti \| **yakṣmaṇā** roga-viśeṣeṇa
**gṛhīto** balād vyāptaḥ saṁs **tamo**'ndhakāraṁ **na kṣiṇoṣi** na
nāśayasi, yataḥ **sthagita-gīḥ** \| **gaditaiḥ**
śrī-danta-kundādi-prakāśataḥ śrī-mukha-śobhādhikyābhiprāyeṇaiva
**mukunda**-śabdaḥ \| bho **indo** ! **no**'smābhiḥ \| anyat tair
vyākhyātam \|

tatra **bho** **indo** iti lekhye \"he\" iti lekhaka-bhramād ity
avagamyate \| bho ity asyaiva vyākhyāyā apekṣyatvād iti \| athavā,
**yathā vayaṁ mukundasya gaditāni** viśeṣeṇa smṛtvā anusandhāya
tad-abhiniveśena **sthagita-giraḥ** **kṣīṇāś** ca nijaga-duḥkhaṁ
sva-buddhy-ādi-raśmibhiḥ kṣapayituṁ na śaknumaḥ, tathā **tvam** apy
asmābhir **lakṣyase** \| ato **yakṣmaṇā gṛhītaḥ kṣīṇaḥ** saṁs **tamaḥ**
sva-bhāryāṇāṁ tārāṇāṁ duḥkhaṁ **nija-dīdhitibhiḥ** sva-kara-sparśādinā
kvacit kiṁ na kṣiṇoṣi ? aho katham atrottaraṁ na yacchasi ? tat **kaccin
mukunda-gaditāni vismṛtya sthagita-gīr** api tathaivāsmābhir
**upalakṣyase** ? evaṁ kaccid ity asyobhayatrāpy anvayaḥ \| anyat
samānam \|\|18\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** nanu, aho yadyapy ete
tiryag-ādyāḥ samudrāntās tad-bhāvād uttarottarādhikyena krośanti, tarhy
ayaṁ sarva-sadguṇaś candramāḥ kathaṁ maunī vartate ? jñātaṁ cedam apīti
bhaṅgī-pūrvakam āhuḥ---**bho indo** ! **tvaṁ balavatā** sudhā-mūrter api
tava parābhavāt praśasta-balena **yakṣmaṇā nigṛhīto'si** \| yataḥ
**kṣīṇaḥ** hīnaḥ san **nijā** yāvatyo **dīdhitayaḥ,** tābhiḥ pūrṇimāyām
api **tamo na kṣiṇoṣi** sūryavat kṣayaṁ prāpayituṁ na śaknoṣi \| **yathā
vayaṁ** śrī-mukunda-viraheṇa **kṣīṇā** nija-duḥkha-haraṇe'py asamarthāḥ,
tathā **tvam** apīty aho tvayy adhika-kaṣṭam eveti bhāvaḥ \| kṣaṇaṁ
parāmṛśyevāhuḥ---**kaccid** iti \| kiṁ vā, **mukundasya gaditāni**
viśleṣārambhe samaya-bandhādīni **vismṛtya**
tad-viraha-bhava-prāgalbhyenāpasmṛtya tad-aniścayenaiva kṣīṇaḥ san
**tamo na kṣiṇoṣi** \| yato vayam iva tvaṁ **sthagita-gīś** ca
**no**'smābhir **upalakṣyase** \| kurary-ādivad ākrośanād etat praśne'py
uttarādānād iti bhāvaḥ \|\|18\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** bhavatu ātmāpaharaṇād asya
tathā-vidhā daśā, induḥ kathaṁ kṣīyamāṇaḥ āsta ity āśaṅkya kācid
āha---**tvaṁ yakṣmaṇā** ity-ādi \| he **indo** ! **balavatā yakṣmaṇā
kṣīṇa iva** kathaṁ **dīdhitibhis tamo na kṣiṇoṣi** ? yakṣma-bādhito jano
yathā kim api kartuṁ na śaknoti, tadvat ko'rthaḥ \| ām, jñātaṁ,
**kaccit** **bho** **yathā vayaṁ** **mukunda-gaditāni** **vismṛtya**
mukundena rahasi yad uktaṁ, tad vismṛtya **sthagitāḥ,** tathā **tvam**
api **sthagita-gīr no**'smābhir **upalakṣyase** \| tat-smaraṇe dhyāyan
kṣiṇoṣi, vayaṁ yathā agre ānandena vismṛtaṁ, paścāt tad-anusmaraṇe
kṣīṇāḥ smaḥ, tathā tvam api \| tad yuktam evaitat \|\|18\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : tvaṁ yakṣmaṇā** iti \|
athavā nedaṁ kāraṇam \| kāraṇaṁ tu jñātam asmābhir ity
āhuḥ---**mukunda-gaditāni vismṛtya** iti \| tasya viśleṣārambhe tena yaḥ
khalv ādhiḥ samayaḥ sa-cāṭu sa-bahu-śapatha-muktas tatra tadānīṁ
vaiklavyātiśayāt tvayā mano na dattam \| ata idānīṁ tāni
**mukunda-gaditāni vismṛtya** mahānutāpād eva **sthagita-gīr
no**'smābhir **upalakṣyase** \| kurary-ādivat ākrośanād etat-praśne'py
uttarādānād iti bhāvaḥ \| **yathā vayam** iti vayam api tad-viśleṣāt
tathā tad-vacana-vismaraṇotthānutāpāt **sthagita-giro** viśīryāma iti
bhāvaḥ \|\|18\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.19 \|\|**

**kiṁ nv ācaritam asmābhir malayānila te'priyam \|**

**govindāpāṅga-nirbhinne hṛdīrayasi naḥ smaram \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** apriyācaraṇaṁ vinā smarodīraṇena
vyathā-jananaṁ he **malayānila** ! tavānucitam ity arthaḥ \|\|19\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** *ity artha*
iti---kṛṣṇa-kṣaṇa-pāteṣu **nirbhinna**-cetasām ārtānām asmākam
akṛta-tvad-aparādhānāṁ punar anyat kāma-vyathotpādanaṁ na yogyam iti
bhāvaḥ \|\|19\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**kaivalya-dīpikā :** **kiṁ nv** iti \| **kim** **apriyam** **ācaritam**
**no hṛdi īrayasi** uddīpayasi \| anena manaḥ-saṅga-lakṣaṇā \|\|19\|\|
\[mu.pha. 12.76\]

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** ebhiḥ saha
kathopakathane svāsthyaṁ na dadāsi, tat **kiṁ te'smābhir apriyam
ācaritam** ? ity āhuḥ---**kiṁ nv** ity-ādi \|\|19\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** rātri-śeṣe vahantaṁ vātam
āsādya tena janitayā kāma-pīḍayāhuḥ---**kim** iti \| **nu** aho \|
katarad **apriyam** \| pāṭhāntare vā-śabdaḥ sa-bhrū-kṣepa-praśne \|
**govindasya** gokulendrasya śrī-gopī-gaṇa-vimohanasya
bhagavato'**pāṅgena** īkṣaṇa-śareṇety arthaḥ \| **niḥ**śeṣatayā
**bhinne** vidārite, asmākaṁ **hṛdi smaram udīrayasi**, kāma-vyathāṁ
janayasīty arthaḥ \|

he **malayānila** ! iti śītala-svabhāvasya te tāpa-jananam etad
anucitam, tatrāpy anya-hatānāṁ punas tvayā hananaṁ paramāyuktam iti
bhāvaḥ \| anyat tair vyākhyātam \|

yad vā, aho bata ! **asmābhiḥ kiṁ** nāma duṣkarma **kṛtam**, yatas
**te** **priyaṁ** nijeṣṭaṁ **smaraṁ** śrī-bhagavad-viṣayakaṁ kāmam
asmākaṁ **hṛdīrayasi**, yato'smākam apy apriyatamasya tat smarasya
tvayoddīpanam ayuktam eveti bhāvaḥ \| tatrāpi svata eva duḥkhitānāṁ
punar duḥkha-jananaṁ naiva yuktam ity āhuḥ---**govinda** iti \| samam
anyat \|\|19\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** rātri-śeṣe mud udvahantaṁ
smaroddīpanaṁ stuti-vyājena nindantya āhuḥ---**kiṁ nv** iti \| tatra
stutir, yathā---he **malayānila** ! malayasya paramārthataḥ
śrīmad-agastya-nivāsasya vyavahārataś candanākarasyānila ! **te** tava
**priyam** **asmābhir nu** aho **kim ācaritam** ? yato **govindasya**
pṛthivyā bhāra-haraṇāya pṛthivyām avatīrṇasyety arthaḥ \| tasya
**apāṅgena** nirbhedakatvāt bāṇa-rūpeṇa **niḥ**śeṣeṇa **bhinne hṛdi**
jīvādhāra-kośe **smaraṁ** smṛtiṁ caitanyam **īrayasi** punaḥ praveśayasi
\| yad vā, **smaraṁ** kāmam api **īrayasi** kim uta caitanyam iti bhāvaḥ
\| yad vā, anilena tvayeraṇān nijānubhavāc ca smarasya vahnitvam
avagamyate \| tatas tan nirbhinnatvān mṛtakatvaṁ prāpte hṛdi
yad-antima-kriyocitaṁ tad-rūpa-vahnim īrayasi dadāsi \| tasmāt kintv
ācaritam ity-ādi \|

atha nindā, yathā he tādṛśa ! **asmābhir** eva tava **apriyaṁ kim
ācaritaṁ,** tad vadety arthaḥ \| **nu** vitarke \| vicāreṇāpi
nāsmad-buddhi-gocaraṁ tad ity arthaḥ \| katham ? tad
āha---tādṛśa-**govindāpāṅga-nirbhinne**'py asmākaṁ tādṛśety-ādi \|
tādṛśaṁ **smaram īrayasi**, tat tu vināpy apriyācaraṇam anya-hatasya,
tatrāpi mriyamāṇasya dāhanaṁ tādṛśasya tava nocitaṁ, tathā
kṣaṇa-vilambāsahatvāt parama-cāpalyaṁ ceti bhāvaḥ \| yad vā, tādṛśe'pi
**hṛdi** kāmam **īrayasi** \| aho tava mūrkhatvaṁ vṛthā
viḍambana-kartṛtvaṁ ceti bhāvaḥ \|\|19\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** kācit tatraiva samaye
meduraṁ vahantam anilam abhimṛśya tad-bādhiteva sāsūyam āha---**kiṁ**
**nv ācaritam** ity-ādi \| he **malayānila** ! **asmābhis te** **kim
apriyam ācaritam** ? na kim apīti cet, katham evaṁ pīḍayasi ? ity
āha---**govindāpāṅga-nirbhinne** **kiṁ smaram īrayasi** prerayasi ?
kṣetre jambīra-rasam iveti śeṣaḥ \| asūyā vyabhicārī \|\|19\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** he **malayānila** ! **te
kim apriyaṁ** vairam **asmābhir ācaritam** ? yad asmin vipat-samaye tvaṁ
vaira-pariśodhanaṁ karoṣīty āhuḥ---**govinda-** iti \|\|19\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.20 \|\|**

**megha śrīmaṁs tvam asi dayito yādavendrasya nūnaṁ**

**śrīvatsāṅkaṁ vayam iva bhavān dhyāyati prema-baddhaḥ \|**

**atyutkaṇṭhaḥ**[^5] **śavala-hṛdayo'smad-vidho bāṣpa-dhārāḥ**

**smṛtvā smṛtvā visṛjasi muhur duḥkhadas tat-prasaṅgaḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : megha** iti \|
ātapārti-haraṇādi-sāmyāt tvaṁ **yādavendrasya nūnaṁ dayitaḥ** sakhāsi,
ato **bhavāṁs taṁ dhyāyati** \| dhyāne liṅgāny āhuḥ---**atyutkaṇṭha**
ity-ādi \| aho kim iti tvayā tena sakhyaṁ kṛtaṁ ? yato **duḥkhadas
tat-prasaṅgaḥ** iti \|\|20\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** kiṁ ca, **megha**
jala-sektṛtvena sarva-tāpāpanodaka **śrīman** vidyud-yuktatvāt, ataḥ
sakhitvāt \| ***taṁ*** yādavendram \| *liṅgāni* jñāpakāni \|
***atyutkaṇṭhas*** tad draṣṭum atīvecchāvān \| **śavala-hṛdayo**
vihvalaḥ \| yathā **vayaṁ** dhyāyāmaḥ, tathā **bhavān** apy
**asmad-vidho**'smat-tulya evārtaḥ \| **bāṣpa-dhārā** aśru-pravāhān \|
**tat-prasaṅgaḥ** śrī-kṛṣṇa-prasaṅgaḥ \|

vastutas tu tvaṁ prema-bhakto'si prahlādādivat tad-dharmāṇāṁ, vāg
gadgadā dravate yasya cittaṁ \[bhā.pu. 11.14.24\] ity-ādīnāṁ tvayi
darśanāt \| tathā ca śrī-kṛṣṇa-saṅgaḥ duḥkhānāṁ sāmsārika-tāpānāṁ
daśā-cchedaka[^6] eva, ata eva sarvasva-tyāga-puraḥsaraṁ
tad-yaśaḥ-śravaṇa-mātreṇa mahānto'raṇyam āpya [tad-dhyānayantas tam itāḥ
\|]{.mark} tad uktaṁ---

> kīrtyamānaṁ yaśo yasya sakṛd ākarṇya rocanam \|
>
> tasmin nyasta-dhiyaḥ pārthāḥ saheran virahaṁ katham \|\| \[bhā.pu.
> 1.10.12\] iti \|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**kaivalya-dīpikā :** **megha** iti \| **śavalaṁ** vyākulam \| atra
smṛtiḥ \|\|20\|\| \[mu.pha. 12.77\]

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) : asmad-vidho vayam iva,**
sādṛśye vidha-pratyayaḥ \|\|20\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** samudrāntike varṣantaṁ
meghaṁ śrī-bhagavad-virahārtyā rudantaṁ matvāhuḥ---**megha** iti \|
vṛṣṭyā bhūmi-secanena lokānāṁ tāpa-haraṇāt, ayaṁ **dayitatve** hetuḥ \|
varṇa-sādṛśyād api dayitatvam āhuḥ---**śrīman** ! he
suśyāma-varṇatvādinā śobhā-yukteti, **yādavendrasya** asmad-dayitasyety
arthaḥ \| yad vā, yādavendratvena yādavā eva tasya dayitatve yogyāḥ,
tathāpi tvam api dayito'sīti bhāvaḥ \|

**nūnaṁ** vitarke \| **śrīvatsāṅkam** asādhāraṇa-lakṣaṇena sarvato
vilakṣaṇam \| yad vā, śrī-yuktāḥ śrī-nanda-vrajasya vatsā aṅke
sneha-lālanādinā sadā kroḍe kṛtā yasya tam \| iti dhyāna-sauṣṭhavāya
gopa-veśādikam abhipretam \| **prema**-pāśena **baddho** **dhyāyati**
cintayati \| **bhavān** iti śrī-bhagavad-dayitatvenādarāt \|

**visṛjasi** iti tvat-prema-vārtayā premodrekāt \| **atyutkaṇṭho**
mahā-vyagraḥ **śavala-hṛdayaś** ca vyākula-manā **asmad-vidhaḥ**, vayam
iva ity arthaḥ \| **smṛtvā smṛtvā** taṁ **muhur bāṣpa-dhārā**
**visṛjasi** muñcasi \| vīpsā muhuḥ-śabdaś ca kathañcid yatnena
smaraṇādau saṁvṛtte'pi punaḥ punas tad-udbhavāt \| **tat-prasaṅgaḥ**
tasminn āsaktiḥ \| kiṁ vā, tasya **prasaṅgaḥ** \| kiṁ tad ? vārtā-
mātram api kiṁ punar dhyānam ity arthaḥ \| anyat tair vyākhyātam \| yad
vā, idam ucitam evety āhuḥ---**duḥkhada** iti \| samam anyat \|\|20\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** atha samudrāntike varṣantaṁ
meghaṁ śrī-bhagavad-virahārtyā rudantaṁ matvā
tat-sārūpya-darśana-jātenākṛtrima-sauhṛdyenāhuḥ---**megha**- iti \|
**nūnaṁ** vitarke \| iti sarvatra vākye yojyam \| he **megha** !
**tvaṁ** **yādavendrasya nūnaṁ dayitaḥ** priya-sakhaḥ **asi** \| yataḥ
he **śrīman** ! prāpta-tat-sārūpya-lakṣmīkaḥ \| tataḥ kim ?
tatrāhuḥ---prāpta-sārūpyād api bhavad-vidhād vilakṣaṇa-lakṣmīkam amuṁ
**bhavān nūnaṁ dhyāyati** \|

nanu prāpte paryanta-phale phalasya vā nyūnatve kiṁ tad-dhyānena ?
tatrāhuḥ---**prema-baddha** iti \| tac chrī-mūrtes tathā svabhāvo yathā
tatra premaiva jñāyate, naudāsīnyaṁ na cerṣyeti bhāvaḥ \|
tatrobhayatrāpi dṛṣṭāntaḥ---**vayam iva** iti \| yasmād evaṁ
**prema-baddhaḥ**, tasmāt **nūnam atyutkaṇṭhaḥ** tena
nirvedādi-nānā-bhāva-**śavala**-citto'py asi \| tatrāpi
hetuḥ---**asmad-vidha** iti \| prema-baddha-tādṛśyāt svānubhavena
jñāyasa ity arthaḥ \|

yad vā, **atyutkaṇṭhatvena** lakṣaṇaṁ **śavala-hṛdayaḥ** śavalaṁ
vaivarṇyena nānā-varṇaṁ hṛdayaṁ madhya-bhāgo yasya tathā-bhūto'sīti \|
tac ca yuktam ity āhuḥ---**asmad-vidha** iti \| aho **nūnam** ata eva
taṁ **smṛtvā smṛtvā** vṛṣṭi-rūpā **bāṣpa-dhārā muhuḥ sṛjasi** sarvatra
vikirasi \| yuktaṁ ca tad ity āhuḥ---**duḥkhada** iti \| **prasaṅga**
āsaktiḥ prastāva-mātraṁ vā \|\|20\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** tatraiva kācin megham
ālokyaiva nigadati---**megha śrīmann** ! ity-ādi \| he **megha** !
**śrīman** ! śrī-yukta ! **tvaṁ yādavendrasya dayito'si** mitram asi
sāvarṇyāt śrīmattvāc ca \| sa śrīmān lakṣmīvān tvam api śobhāvān ity
arthaḥ \| **nūnaṁ** manye **vayam iva bhavān** api **śrīvatsāṅkaṁ
prema-baddhaḥ** san **dhyāyati** \| prema-baddhatvaṁ vyākaroti---**api**
ity-ādi \| **api** sambhāvanāyām \| **utkaṇṭha** utkaṇṭhāvān udgrīvo vā
**śavala-hṛdayo** nānā-bhāva-śāvalya-valita-manā bhūtvā **bāṣpa-dhārā**
visṛjasi, **muhuḥ** **asmad-vidhaḥ** asmat-sadṛśaḥ, sādṛśye
vidha-pratyayaḥ \| kiṁ kṛtvā ? **smṛtvā** tat-premānukṣaṇa-smaraṇena
ucitam evaitat \| katham ? ity āha---**duḥkhadas tat-prasaṅgaḥ** \|
tat-prastāva-mātram api duḥkhadaṁ, kim uta nirantarānusmaraṇam iti
\|\|20\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : dayitaḥ** sakhā \| **tvam
asi prema-baddhaḥ** prāpta-bandhanaḥ san, **taṁ dhyāyati śrīvatsāṅkam**
iti \| tasya ca varṇena sāmye'pi tasya śrīvatsāṅko'dhika iti tatra
tavāśakti-kāraṇam avagatam iti bhāvaḥ \| **śavala-hṛdayaḥ**
viṣāda-malina-cetāḥ vṛṣṭi-miṣeṇa **bāṣpa-dhārāḥ visṛjasi** vṛṣṭi-miṣeṇa
rodiṣi \| aho kim iti tvayā tatrāsaktiḥ kṛtā, yatas **tat-prasaṅgo
duḥkhada** eva \|\|20\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.21 \|\|**

**priya-rāva-padāni bhāṣase**

**mṛta-sañjīvikayānayā girā \|**

**karavāṇi kim adya te priyaṁ**

**vada me valgita-kaṇṭha kokila \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** he **kokila** ! me
**priya-rāvasya** priyaṁ-vadasya śrī-kṛṣṇasya padānīva **padāni**
śabdāṁs tvaṁ **bhāṣase** \| **mṛtān sañjīvayati** iti tathā tayā
**anayā** komalayā **girā** **valgita-kaṇṭha** ramaṇīya-kaṇṭha me
kathaya **kiṁ tava priyaṁ karavāṇi ?** iti \|\|21\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** priyaṁ rauti vadatīti
**priya-rāvaḥ,** tasya \| **valgitaṁ** priya-ramyayoḥ iti \|\|21\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**kaivalya-dīpikā :** **priya-** iti \| **priyasya** nāma **padāni** iti
\| **bhāṣase** **anayā** apaśyam a-svara-yuktyā \| **valgito**
valgīkṛtaḥ \| atra guṇa-kīrtanam \|\|21\|\| \[mu.pha. 12.78\]

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** tatra kāścit
pika-ravam ākarṇya kṛṣṇa-svaraṁ smṛtvā vadanti---**priya-rāva-** ity-ādi
\| **priyasya** śrī-kṛṣṇasya rāvavad **rāvo** yasya \| **rāva-padāni**
ity ekaṁ vā padam \|\|21\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** rātri-śeṣe kūjana-kokilam
āhuḥ---**priya-** iti \| tad-viraheṇa **mṛtān** janāṁs
tat-smara-sadṛśatayā tan-naikaṭya-bodhane **samyag jīvayati** iti tayā
**girā** hetunā **tava** **priyaṁ kiṁ karavāṇi** ? api tu na kiñcit
kartuṁ śaknuyām ity arthaḥ \| **valgitaḥ** pañcama-svareṇa valgūkṛtaḥ
**kaṇṭho** yena, tat-sambodhanam \| anena śrī-bhagavad-gīḥ-sāmyārthaṁ
susvaratvaṁ sūcayanti \| atra ca **karavāṇi** iti **me** iti
caikatva-nirdeśaḥ \| śrī-bhagavad-vāṅ-mādhurī-hṛta-cittāyāḥ kasyāścid
ekasyā vokteḥ \| yad vā, sarvāsām api pratyekaṁ tādṛśokter eva \| anyat
tair vyākhyātam \|

yad vā, **anayā** śrī-bhagavad-gīḥ-sadṛśyā **girā** tathā-bhūtayā
**samyag jīvatīti** sa-jīvaḥ, mṛto bhavati sañjīvo'pi yathā, tayā kiṁ
katarad **apriyam** aniṣṭaṁ **karavāṇi** kurvaty asmi, yatas tvaṁ tu me
mayi **vada** kūja, kūjasīty arthaḥ \| tac ca tvat-svabhāvād evety
āśayena sambodhayati---**valgita-kaṇṭha** ! he śavala-kaṇṭheti ! ayaṁ
premārty-ukti-viśeṣaḥ \| yad vā, **anayāpi girā** tava **apriyaṁ kiṁ
karavāṇi**, api tu naiva kariṣyāmīty arthaḥ \| nijābhīṣṭe maraṇe
sahāyatvāt \| ato **vada** \| samam anyat \|\|21\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** atha rātry-avasāne kūjantaṁ
kokilaṁ pūrvavat stuti-nindābhyām āhuḥ---**priya-rāva-** iti \| tatra
stutiḥ---he **kokila** ! pañcama-gāna-prasiddha ! tatrāpi **valgitaḥ**
priyeṇaiva śikṣā-viśeṣād valgu-kṛtaḥ **kaṇṭho** yasya, he tathā-vidha !
**priyasya rāva** iva rāvaḥ pañcama-svaro yatra, tādṛśāni **padāni**
gīta-nibaddhān śabdān **bhāṣase** \| yad vā, **priyasya rāvaḥ**
śikṣā-vacanaṁ yeṣu, tādṛśāni **padāni** dūtyānurūpān śabdān **bhāṣase**
\| tatas tan-naikaṭya-bodhanena tad-viraha-mṛtān **samyag jīvayati** iti
tathā tathā **girā** hetunā **kiṁ priyaṁ karavāṇi** tan **me** mahyaṁ
**vada** \| kṛpayā jñāpaya \| atraika-vacanaṁ pratyekam api
tat-kṣamatā-vivakṣayā pṛthag-ukteḥ \|

atha nindā---he cañcala-**kaṇṭha** ! **kokila** ! **mṛta-sañjīvikayā**
tathā **girā** hetunā **priyasya rāvaḥ** śikṣā yatra, tādṛśāni **padāni
bhāṣase** \| mayā tad-virahāsahiṣṇutvāj jīvanān maraṇam eva varaṁ
manyate, tat tu sa iva tvam apy āpātato'mṛtāyamāna-vacanena madhye
madhye vighātayan duḥkhada evāsīd iti bhāvaḥ \| tasmāt **tavāpriyaṁ**
tuṇḍa-troṭanādikam atrāparādhe **kiṁ karavāṇi** tat tvam eva **vada**
sva-daṇḍa-viśeṣaṁ svayam evānumanyasva, anyathāparādha-kṣayo na bhaved
iti bhāvaḥ \|\|21\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** tatraiva kācit pika-ravam
ākarṇya prīyamāṇāha---**priya-rāva** ity-ādi \| he **kokila** ! **adya
kiṁ te priyaṁ karavāṇi** ? **vada** katham akāṇḍe naḥ priyaṁ bhavatyā
kāryam ity āha---he **priya-rāva** ! priyasya rāva iva rāvo yasya, sa
tathā he tathā-bhūta ! **mṛta-sañjīvikayā** mṛta-sañjīvinyā **anayā girā
padāni bhāṣase** \| yad vā, priyasya śrī-kṛṣṇasya rāvavat padānīrayase
katham atra padaṁ ? he **valgita-kaṇṭha** ! cañcala-kaṇṭha ! \|\|21\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** he **priya-rāva kokila**
! **anayā padāni** asmad-viraha-duḥkha-trāṇāny eva **bhāṣase**, padaṁ
vyavasita-trāṇa-sthāna-lakṣmāṅghri-vastuṣu ity amaraḥ \| **valgitaḥ**
valgūkṛtaḥ **kaṇṭho** yena, he tādṛśa ! atra virahe kokila-śabdasya
duḥkhadatvāt, priya-rāvety-ādyāḥ sarvā eva viparīta-lakṣaṇayā vakroktaya
eva \| tena sva-śabdena māṁ jvālayatas **tava kiṁ priyaṁ karavāṇi** ?
tuṇḍam eva dhakṣyāmīti bhāvaḥ \|\|21\|\|

**\...**

**\|\|** **10.90.22 \|\|**

**na calasi na vadasy udāra-buddhe**

**kṣiti-dhara cintayase mahāntam artham \|**

**api bata vasudeva-nandanāṅghriṁ**

**vayam iva kāmayase stanair vidhartum \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** he **kṣiti-dhara** ! tvaṁ **na
vadasi** **na calasi** \| ato nūnaṁ **mahāntam arthaṁ cintayase** \|
**bata** tarhi \| **api** kiṁ, yathā **stanair vidhartuṁ vayaṁ**
kāmayāmahe, tathā tvaṁ stana-tulyaiḥ śṛṅgair voḍhuṁ **kāmayase** \| om
iti cet, tarhi tavāpy asmad-avasthā bhaviṣyatīti bhāvaḥ \|\|22\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** *stana-tulyais*
tīkṣṇāgraiḥ \| *om iti cet* satyaṁ taṁ dhartum icchāmīti yadi vadasi \|
*iti bhāva* iti---nirasta-samastaihikāmuṣmikāḥ satyas tad-ekatānās tathā
tvam api kṛtārtho bhaviṣyasīty āśayaḥ \|\|22\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**kaivalya-dīpikā :** **na** iti \| **api** aho \| yathā **vayaṁ**
**stanair vidhartuṁ** kāmayāmahe \| atra trapā-nāśaḥ \|\|22\|\|
\[mu.pha. 12.79\]

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** anyāḥ ūcuḥ---**na
calasi** ity-ādi \| **tvaṁ** sāvadhānā api yad evaṁ karoṣi, tad
avagataṁ, **vayam iva** iti **stana**-prāyaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ \|\|22\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** mahā-sthiraṁ rātrau
prāyaḥ śayita-sarva-jantutvāt tūṣṇīṁ sthitaṁ cāruṇodaye śrī-raivatakaṁ
dṛṣṭvāhuḥ---**na** iti \| he **udāra-buddhe** ! iti mahāśayasya tad evaṁ
yuktam eveti \| tathā he **kṣiti-dhara** ! iti \| atas tvayaiva pṛthvī
rakṣiteti bhāvaḥ \| mahārtha-cintanam eva vitarkayanti---**api** iti \|
**vasudeva-nandanasya** parama-mohanasya bhagavato'**ṅghriṁ** pādaṁ
**vi**śeṣeṇa premāliṅganādinā **dhartum** \| anyat tair vyākhyātam \|

tatra mūla-sthitasya **na calasi** ity-āder utkrameṇa lekho
lekhaka-bhramāt \| kiṁ vā, mahārtha-cintanena calana-mātrasyāpy abhāvena
tan-māhātmyāpekṣayā tathaiva vyākhyāpatter iti \|\|22\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** mahā-sthiraṁ rātrau prāyaḥ
śayita-sarva-jantutvāt tūṣṇīṁ sthitaṁ cāruṇodaye śrī-raivatakaṁ
dṛṣṭvāhuḥ---**na** iti \| he **kṣiti-dhara** ! yadyapi
pañcāśat-koṭi-yojana-vistīrṇāṁ pṛthvīṁ dharasi, tathāpi **na calasi,**
**na** ca **vadasi** \| tasmād eva he **udāra-buddhe** ! mahā-citta !
tad eva darśayanti---kam api **mahāntam arthaṁ** puruṣārthaṁ
**cintayase** cintayasi \| **kāmayase** iti \| tatrāpi sa-śaṅkam āhuḥ \|
**api** praśne \| **bata** khede \| sa ca mahārtho mata-bhedān
nānā-vidha iti \| tatra **devasya** asmat-pūjyasya śvaśurasya yo
**nandanaḥ** pradhāna-putro'smat-patir ity arthaḥ \| ārya-putra itivat
spaṣṭatayā anuktir lajjayā \| tasya **vasu** parama-dhana-rūpam
**aṅghriṁ** vayam api **stanair** **vidhartuṁ** svayaṁ nārīyamāṇaḥ
stanīkṛtaiḥ śṛṅgair āliṅgituṁ kiṁ **kāmayase** ? yadi kāmayase,
tadāsmākam iva tavāpi buddhi-hīnatvaṁ sva-prāṇa-mātre'pi
dhāraṇā-sāmarthyaṁ bhaviṣyasīty arthaḥ \| stanānāṁ bahutva-nirdeśas tu
tasya lobhātiśayaṁ dyotayati \| atra **vasu-deva**-padayor
bhinna-kramatayā prayuktayor apy ekatra santāpena
śvaśura-nāmoccāraṇa-pramāda unmādoktyā na doṣāya iti jñeyam \| ṭīkāyāṁ
**na calasi na vadasy** anayor vyutkrama-nirdeśaḥ prāyo lekhaka-bhramād
iti \|\|22\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** tadaiva kācit raivatam
anusmṛtya nigadati---**na calasi** ity-ādi \| he **udāra-buddhe** !
**kṣiti-dhara** ! **na calasi na vadasi,** ko'rthaḥ ? āṁ jñātaṁ,
**mahāntam arthaṁ** prayojanaṁ **cintayase**, tad eva brūhīty
āha---**api bata** ity-ādi \| **api** sambhāvane, **bata** khede \|
**vasudeva-nandanāṅghriṁ stanaiḥ** stana-prāyaiḥ śikharair **vidhartuṁ
kāmayase** \| **vayam iva** vayaṁ yathā stanair voḍhuṁ kāmayamānā
nirantaraṁ kam apy arthaṁ cintayāmaḥ, tvaṁ puruṣo bhūtvāpi strī-bhāvam
āsādya **kāmayasa** iti nigarvaḥ \|\|22\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** he **kṣiti-dhara** !
raivataka-parvata ! nūnaṁ tvaṁ **mahāntam arthaṁ** svābhīpsitaṁ
**cintayasi**, ato **bata** iti idaṁ vā tavābhīpsitam ity arthaḥ \|
**vayaṁ** yathā **stanair** **dhartuṁ** kāmayāmahe, tathā tvaṁ stanaiḥ
kiṁ voḍhuṁ **kāmayase** ? om iti cet, tarhi tavāpy asmad-avasthā
bhaviṣyatīti bhāvaḥ \|\|22\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.23 \|\|**

**śuṣyad-dhradāḥ karaśitā**[^7] **bata sindhu-patnyaḥ**

**sampraty apāsta**[^8]**-kamala-śriya iṣṭa-bhartuḥ \|**

**yadvad vayaṁ madhu-pateḥ praṇayāvalokam**

**aprāpya muṣṭa-hṛdayāḥ puru-karśitāḥ sma \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** bhoḥ **sindhu-patnyo** nadyaḥ !
samprati grīṣme sindhur megha-dvārā amṛta-vṛṣṭyā yuṣmān nānandayati \|
**bata** aho kaṣṭam \| ataḥ **śuṣyanto hradā** yāsāṁ tāḥ \|
**apagata-kamala-śobhāḥ** kṛśāś ca **vayaṁ** **yathā** priyatamasya
**bhartur madhu-pateḥ** \| **sma** prasiddham \|\|23\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** **kṛśāni taṭāni** kūlāni
yāsāṁ tāḥ \| kvacit \"kara-śitā\" iti pāṭhe tu guṇādeśas tv ārṣa eva \|
ata ānandābhāvāt \| **śuṣyat**-toyā vigata-jalā **hradā** snānādy-arthaṁ
janāvataraṇa-sthānāni \| **madhu-pater** yadu-pateḥ **muṣṭa-hṛdayāḥ**
hṛṣṭa-cetasaḥ\| **puru** adhikaṁ, puruḥ puroge pracure
svarloka-nṛpa-bhedayoḥ iti haimaḥ \|\|23\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**kaivalya-dīpikā :** he **sindhu-patnyaḥ** ! mahā-nadyaḥ ! āḥ kaṣṭam \|
yūyaṁ sūrpasthā bhavathaḥ \| **śuṣyanto** **hradā** hṛdaya-sthānīyāḥ
pradeśā yāsāṁ tāḥ \| **apetāḥ kamala-śriyo** sukhāyamāna-padma-śobhā
yāsāṁ, tās tathā \| **vayam** apy evaṁ-vidhāḥ \| atra tanutā \|\|23\|\|
\[mu.pha. 12.80\]

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** evaṁ **śuṣyad-dhradā**
ity-ādi \| yuṣmākaṁ bhartāpi niṣṭanase, yūyam api viraha-**karśitā** ity
arthaḥ \|\|23\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** grīṣme kṛśāḥ, tatrāpi
rātrau mudrita-kamalatvena śobhā-hīnā nadīr dūrato dṛṣṭvā tāḥ paramārtā
matvāhuḥ---**śuṣyad** iti \|

**iṣṭas** tad-anyasyeṣṭatvābhāvena parama-priyaś cāsau **bhartā** svāmī
ceti \| tathā tasyeti tasyāsmat-paripālanaṁ yuktam eveti bhāvaḥ \|

**madhupater** nijāśeṣa-guṇādi-prakaṭanārthaṁ yadu-kule'vatīrya
tac-chreṣṭatāṁ gatasya, tathāpi yādavān eva pālayati, na tv asmān iti
bhāvaḥ \| ata eva yena **avalokam** apy **aprāpya muṣṭa-hṛdayā**
naṣṭa-cittāḥ **puru** yuṣmatto'py adhikaṁ **karśitāḥ** kārśyaṁ prāpitā
vartāmahe \| atra hradānām āntaratayā hṛdaya-tulyatvādinā
**muṣṭa-hṛdayā** ity asya pratipadaṁ dārṣṭāntike **śuṣyad-dhradā** iti
jñeyam \| ato'**peta-kamala-śriya** ity uktyā dṛṣṭānte'py atra
mlanatvādināpeta-mukhābja-śobhā iti dhvanitam eva \| anyat tair
vyākhyātam \|

tatra sindhu-megha-dvārety-ādikaṁ dṛṣṭānte **praṇayāvalokam aprāpya**
ity asya dhvany-anusārāt **karśitā** ity asyaiva vyākhyā \| kṛśāś ceti
tathā **iṣṭa-bhartur** ity asyaiva priyatamasya bhartur iti \| athavā,
**iṣṭa-bhartuḥ** sindhor eva hetoḥ, tat-kṛtopekṣayā **śuṣyad-dhradā**
ity-ādi \| anyat samānam \|\|23\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** atha nidāghe kṣudṛā nadīr
dūrato dṛṣṭvā tāś ca mūrcchitā matvā pūrva-pūrvavad asambodhya mitha
āhuḥ---**śuṣyad** iti \| **bata** vismaye khede vā \| **sindhor** api
**patnya** etāḥ samprati **apeta-kamalam** iva mukha-**śriyo** jātāḥ,
tathā **śuṣyanto hradās** tad-rūpa-**hṛdayāni** yāsāṁ, tathā-bhūtāś ca
jātāḥ \| kiṁ kṛtvā ? **iṣṭo bhartā** ca yaḥ sindhuḥ, tasya
**praṇayāvalokaṁ** virahātmanā nidāghenaiva vicchedanād **aprāpya,** tad
aho asmat-sādṛśyam etā api gatā iti mlāna-mukham āhuḥ---**yadvad vayam**
iti \| tataḥ **puru-karśitā** iti puru-śabdenāpeta-mukha-śrītvam apy
antar-bhāvitam \|\|23\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** nanu bho **nadyaḥ** !
kṣiti-dharo grāva-mayo'pi puruṣaḥ sann api yad aṅghriṁ stanair voḍhuṁ
kāmayate, strī-bhāvam urarīkṛtya vakṣasi kartum abhilaṣati,
tad-anucintayā striyo bhavatyo yadīdṛśāṁ yāsyanti, tat kiṁ citram ? ity
āhuḥ---**śuṣyad-dhradā** ity-ādiḥ \| yataḥ, bho **sindhu-patnyaḥ** !
mahājana-gṛhiṇyaḥ ! **iṣṭa-bhartuḥ** śrī-kṛṣṇasya, sindhus tāvad
upapati-mātram, iṣṭa-bhartā tu vo nūnaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇa eva \| atas tasya
**madhupateḥ** **praṇayāvalokam aprāpya** **muṣṭa-hṛdayāḥ**
**puru-karśitāḥ** khinnā atyanta-kṛśā bhavatyaḥ santi \| yat
**śuṣyad-dhradā** śuṣyan hradā iva hṛdo gambhīrataraṁ **hṛdayaṁ** yāsāṁ,
ata eva **karśitāḥ** khinnāḥ \| kheda-liṅgam āha---**samprati** idānīm
**apetāḥ kamalānāṁ** kamala-prāyāṇāṁ mukhānāṁ **śriyo** yāsām \| kā iva
? ity āha---**yadvad vayaṁ** **smaḥ**, vayaṁ yathā śuṣyan manaso
mlānānanāḥ khinnāḥ **puru-kṛśāś** cety arthaḥ \|\|23\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** bhoḥ **sindhu-patnyo**
nadyaḥ ! **samprati** yūyaṁ **śuṣyad-dhradāḥ** stha \| tatra kāraṇam
āhuḥ---**iṣṭa-bhartuḥ** **sindhu-patnīnām** api yo'bhīṣṭa-sukha-prado
bhartā yadupatiḥ, tasya **praṇayāvalokam aprāpya** eva **yadvad vayaṁ**
praṇayāvalokam aprāpya **muṣṭa-hṛdayāḥ** vañcita-cittāḥ smaḥ, tadvad eva
yūyam \|\|23\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.24 \|\|**

**haṁsa svāgatam āsyatāṁ piba payo brūhy aṅga śaureḥ kathāṁ**

**dūtaṁ tvāṁ nu vidāma**[^9] **kaccid ajitaḥ svasty āsta uktaṁ purā \|**

**kiṁ vā naś cala-sauhṛdaḥ smarati taṁ kasmād bhajāmo vayaṁ**

**kṣaudrālāpaya kāmadaṁ**[^10] **śriyam ṛte saivaika-niṣṭhā striyām
\|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** tadaiva daivād āgataṁ haṁsaṁ
dūtaṁ kalpayitvāhuḥ---**haṁsa** iti \| **no**'smān prati **purā** rahasy
**uktam** **kiṁ vā cala-sauhṛdaḥ smarati** ?

smṛtvaiva māṁ prasthāpitavān iti ced ata āhuḥ---he **kṣaudra** !
kṣudrasya dūta ! **kasmāt taṁ vayaṁ bhajāmaḥ** ?

kāmārtham āhvayati yuṣmān iti ced ata āhuḥ---aho tarhi **tam**
**ālāpaya** ākāraya \| om iti gacchantam iva taṁ punar āhuḥ---yāsmān
vañcayitvā ekākinī sevate, tāṁ **śriyam ṛte** **tam** eva **ālāpaya** \|

**sā** tad-**eka-niṣṭhā** kathaṁ parihartuṁ śakyate ? iti ced ata
āhuḥ---**striyām**, jātāv eka-vacanam \[?\]\| asmāsu strīṣu madhye kiṁ
**saivaika-niṣṭhā**, na tu vayam ? ity arthaḥ \|

pāṭhāntare tu, **kṣaudraṁ** madhu, tadvan madhurālāpa-mātraṁ yasya,
**tam akāmadam** arati-pradaṁ **śriyam ṛte vayaṁ kasmād bhajāmaḥ** ?
kintv anādṛtāpi satī punaḥ punaḥ saiva bhajatu yato'smādṛṣyo māninyaḥ
striya **eka-niṣṭhā** ekatraiva sva-saṁmāna-siddhau niṣṭhā yāsām iti
\|\|24\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** **svāgataṁ** suṣṭhv
āgamanaṁ jātam \| **āsyatām** upaviśyatām \| **payaḥ** kṣīram \|
**cala-sauhṛdaḥ,** ato'trāhuḥ---**taṁ** śaurim \| *ity artha*
iti---**vayam** api tad-**eka-niṣṭhā** eveti \| tasyehāgamanam ucitam
eva bhakta-vātsalyād iti bhāvaḥ \| pāṭhāntare \"kṣaudrālāpam akāmadam"
iti pāṭhe tu kṣudrā madhumakṣikāḥ, tābhir niṣpāditaṁ kṣaudram \|\|24\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**kaivalya-dīpikā :** **haṁsa** iti \| he **haṁsa** ! **āsyatām**
upaviśyatām \| **śaureḥ** kṛṣṇasya \| **nu** aho ! **ajitaḥ** kṛṣṇaḥ \|
**purā** pūrvam asmān prati yad **uktaṁ**, tat **kiṁ smarati** ? **taṁ**
ca **kasmād bhajāmo vayam** \| yato'sau **kṣaudravad** madhuvan
madhurālāpo na tu **kāmadaḥ** \| **śriyam ṛte** **sā** hi yāsāṁ strīṇāṁ
madhye **eka-niṣṭhā** ekasminn eva sthirībhūtā, na tu cañcaleti
sotprāsoktiḥ \| ayam arthaḥ---acañcalā apy asmān ujjhitvā cañcalāṁ
śriyaṁ sa bhajate iti \| atronmādaḥ \| mahiṣyaḥ kurary-ādīn \|\|

atra ca smṛti-guṇa-kīrtana-vyādhi-pralāpāś catasro daśāḥ
kāvya-prakāśa-niṣṭhāḥ[^11] \| nidrā-cchedādayas tu ṣaṭ nayana-prītir ity
atra rati-rahasyasthā[^12] darśitā iti jñeyam \| tāsāṁ
nānā-mahiṣī-gatatvād yat kramād uktāḥ \| mṛti-lakṣaṇā tv anyā
smara-daśāsti \| sā ca---

itīdṛśena bhāvena kṛṣṇe yogeśvareśvare \|

dhriyamāṇena mādhavyo lebhire vaiṣṇavīṁ gatim \|\| \[bhā.pu. 10.90.25\]

ity anena mūla-granthena sūcitāpy amaṅgalatvād iha noktāḥ \|
ekādaśa-śloke jala-keli-prasaṅge mūle darśitā \| tatra ca sannihite'pi
bhagavati tad-ālāpa-sauṣṭhavena tāsāṁ vaicittyāvirbhāvān nāsya bhedasya
pūrvānurāgādiṣv antarbhāvaḥ śakyo vaktum \| tathā ca tatroktaṁ---

kṛṣṇasyaivaṁ viharato gaty-ālāpekṣita-smitaiḥ \|

narma-kṣveli-pariṣvaṅgaiḥ strīṇāṁ kila hṛtā dhiyaḥ \|\|

ūcur mukundaika-dhiyo gira unmatta-vaj jaḍam \|

cintayantyo'ravindākṣaṁ tāni me gadataḥ śṛṇu \|\| \[bhā.pu.
10.90.13-14\]

na cāsminn adhyāye bhagavato vyavadhānādikam uktam \| tasmād
vaicittya-rūpaṁ vipralambhasya bhedāntaram avaśyam abhyupetavyam \| ayam
evātra vidagdha-buddher ācāryasyābhiprāyaḥ \|\|\|\|24\|\| \[mu.pha.
12.81\]

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** kāścit sammukhe daivād
āgataṁ haṁsam ālokya dūtatvena paribhāvya vadanti---haṁsety-ādi \| he
**haṁsa** ! **svāgatam āsyatāṁ**, gamanāgamanābhyāṁ śrānto'si \| **payaḥ
piba** \| pītvā viśramya **śaureḥ kathāṁ** **brūhi** \| **tvāṁ dūtam
anuvidāma** \| **kaccid ajitaḥ svasty āste** ? **uktaṁ purā** yadyapi
\"svasty āste\" iti pūrvoktaṁ, tathāpy utkaṇṭhayā pṛcchāma iti bhāvaḥ \|

**kiṁ vā, no**'smān **smarati**, tatra kaḥ sandehaḥ ?
tatrāhuḥ---**cala-sauhṛda** iti smaraṇād bhāva-vyañjakaṁ **taṁ
cala-sauhṛdaṁ** **vayaṁ bhajāmaḥ** \|

kasmāt ? iti svayam eva hetum upanyasya striyo'nabhijñāś ced iti
siddhāntayanti---śrīr api \| śrīḥ sā kathaṁ bhajati ?
tatrāhuḥ---**śriyam ṛte** śriyaṁ vinā śriyo vārtā tyajyatāṁ, **sā** tu
kevalam **eka-niṣṭhā** ekasmin vakṣasi sthāne niṣṭhā nitarām avasthānaṁ
yasyā, ataḥ sā strī na bhavati, aṅga-viśeṣa eva seti tātparyam \|
**kṣaudraṁ** madhu tad iva **ālāpa** eva yasya **akāmadam**
anabhīpsitadam \| \"kṣaudrālāpaya\" iti pāṭhe svāmi-kṛto vārthaḥ \|
unmāda-bhāvo'yaṁ vaicittya-bhāvāntar-gataḥ \|\|24\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** prātar āgataṁ haṁsaṁ
dūtaṁ matvāhuḥ---**haṁsa** iti \| **svāgatam** iti suṣṭhv āgataṁ kim ity
abhyāgataṁ prati svāgata-praśnasya yogyatvāt \| yad vā, sad-avasare'smin
yat tvayātrāgataṁ, tac chobhanam ity arthaḥ \| ata **āsyatām**
upaviśyatāṁ, **payaḥ** kṣīraṁ **piba** ca \| evam ātithyena sammānya
prārthayante---**brūhi** iti \| **aṅga** ! iti sādara-sambodhane \| kiṁ
vā, asmākam aṅga-tulya ! he paramātmīya ! ity arthaḥ \| **śaureḥ**
kṛpayā śūra-vaṁśe jātasya asmad-bhartuḥ **kathāṁ** kuśala-vārtāṁ kiñcid
vṛttaṁ vā **brūhi** \| tac ca yuktam evety āhuḥ---**nu** niścitaṁ,
**tvā** tvāṁ **dūtaṁ** **vidāma** vidma iti \|

tatrādau kuśalaṁ pṛcchanti---**kaccid** iti \| **svasti** sukham \|
**ajitaḥ** premṇā na kenacid api vaśīkṛta ity arthaḥ \| eṣā
praṇaya-kopoktiḥ \|

nanu devyo bhavatīnāṁ viraheṇāsau kathaṁ sukham āstām ? iti cet, tarhi
**purā** pūrvam anunayādinā **naḥ** praty **uktaṁ** **kiṁ vā**
**smarati** \| **kiṁ vā** ity eka-padam eva vā, sa-bhrū-bhaṅga-praśne
kiṁ nv ity-ādivat \| yad vā, **puroktaṁ** **no**'smān **vā kiṁ smarati**
?

nanu tad eva sevā-parā yuṣmān kṛtajño'sau smaraty eveti cet, tatra na
viśvasima ity āhuḥ---**cala-sauhṛdo**'sthira-premeti \|

nanu tat-priyatamāḥ ! sthira-sauhṛdo'sau yuṣmān kila kāmayate \| tatra
sa-mānam āhuḥ---**tam** iti \|

nanu, tad-virahārtaḥ kāmado'sau bhoktuṁ yujyata eveti cet, tarhi tam
atraiva **ālāpaya** \| ekasminn eva niṣṭhā dṛḍha-sthiratā yasyāḥ sā \|
anyat tair vyākhyātam \|

tatra yuṣmākam ājñeti yathā yuṣmad-ājñā syād ity arthaḥ \| yad vā,
yuṣmān iti lekhye yuṣmad-ājñeti lekhaka-bhramād iti \|

athavā **striyāṁ** strīṣu madhye **sā evaika-niṣṭhā** evāsminn eva
susthirā, na tu cañcaleti sotprāsoktiḥ \| aho tad-eka-niṣṭhā asmān hitvā
cañcalāṁ yo bhajate, **taṁ** kuto **vayaṁ bhajema** iti bhāvaḥ \| anyat
samam \|

evaṁ śrī-bhagavatā sākṣād virājamānena saṁyoge vidyamāne'pi
prema-viśeṣodrekeṇa tat-svabhāvaja-vaicitryād virahavat kvacid
dainyoktiḥ, atas tādṛśa-premaiva śrī-bhagavad-vaśī-karaṇāya bhavati \|
kintu virahārti-mayatve'pi tasya parama-puruṣārthatvaṁ śrī-bhāgavatāmṛte
bahu vivṛtam eva \|\|24\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** prātar āgataṁ haṁsaṁ dūtaṁ
matvāhuḥ---he **haṁsa** iti\| **svāgatam** iti \| suṣṭhu āgataṁ kim ity
arthaḥ \| yad vā, sad-avasare yat svayam āgataṁ tac chobhanam ity arthaḥ
\| tataś ca **āsyatām** upaviśyatāṁ, **payaḥ** kṣīraṁ **piba** \|

evam ātithyena sambhāvya prārthayante---**brūhi** iti \| **aṅga** iti
sādara-sambodhane \| kiṁ vā, asmākam aṅga-tulya ! he paramātmīya ! ity
arthaḥ \| **śaureḥ** śūrasya vaṁśe kenāpi sarveṣāṁ bhāgyena jātasya
asmad-bhartuḥ **kathāṁ** samudācāraṁ **brūhi** \| tac ca yuktam evety
āhuḥ---**nu** niścitaṁ **tvā** tvāṁ **dūtaṁ vidāma** vidma iti \|

tatrādau kuśalaṁ pṛcchanti---**kaccid** iti \| **svasti** sukham
**ajitaḥ** premṇā na kenacid api vaśīkṛta ity arthaḥ \| ity
antar-īrṣyābhivyaktiḥ \|

nanu devyo bhavatīnāṁ viraheṇāsau kathaṁ sukham āstām ? iti cet, tarhi
**purā** pūrvam anunayādi-samaye **naḥ** praty **uktaṁ**, **kiṁ vā
smarati** ? **kiṁvā** ity eka-padam eva vā \| sa-bhrū-bhaṅga-praśne kiṁ
nv ity-ādivat \| yad vā, **puroktaṁ no**'smān **vā kiṁ smarati** ?

nanu tad-eka-sevā-parā yuṣmān kṛtajño'sau smaraty eva ? iti cet, tatra
na viśvasima ity āhuḥ---**cala-sauhṛdaḥ** asthira-premeti \|

nanu tat-priyatamāḥ ! sthira-sauhṛdo'sau yuṣmān kila kāmayate \| tatra
samānam āhuḥ---**tam** iti \|

nanu, tad-virahārtaḥ kāmado'sau bhajanīya eveti cet, tarhi tam atraiva
**ālāpaya** \| atra tad-dhitāntatvenānyathā prāptatvān na sākṣāc
chvasura-pitur nāma-grahaṇaṁ śaṅkyam \| anyat tu tatra **eka-niṣṭhā**
iti ekasminn eva niṣṭhā dṛḍha-sthiratā yasyāḥ **sā** iti kākūktiḥ
yuṣmad-ājñeti \| atra yathā yuṣmākam ājñā syād ity arthaḥ \| yad vā,
yuṣmān iti lekhye lekhaka-bhrama iti \|\|24\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** atraiva kācit purataḥ
samāgacchantaṁ haṁsam ālokyāha---**haṁsa-** ity-ādi \| he **haṁsa** !
**svāgataṁ** sukhenāgatam **āsyatām** \| ehi ehi, **payaḥ** kṣīraṁ
**piba** \|

nanu katham akāṇḍe mayi tavāyam ādaraḥ ? ity āha---**brūhi** ity-ādi \|
he **aṅga** ! **kathāṁ brūhi** \|

tat kathām ahaṁ na jānāmi \| kathaṁ brūyām ? ity āha---**dūtam** ity-ādi
\| **nu** bhoḥ \| **tvāṁ dūtaṁ vidāma** \|

satyaṁ dūta evāsmi \| kaṁ vaktavyaṁ brūhīty āha---**kaccid** ity-ādi \|
**ajitaḥ kaccit svasti āste** ? **āsta** iti yadyapi purā āste iti
pūrvoktaṁ, tathāpi bhūyo vadeti bhāvaḥ \| kiṁ vā, **no**'smān
**smarati**, tatra kaḥ sandehaḥ ? ity āha---**cala-sauhṛdaḥ**
asthira-premānanusmaraty eva \| tasmād yūyaṁ taṁ bhajatety
āha---**kasmāt taṁ bhajāmo vayam** ?

nanu kas tasyāparādhaḥ ? ity āha---**kṣaudrālāpaṁ** kṣaudraṁ madhu
tadvat ālāpa eva yasya, na tu madhurāśayaṁ, tatrāpi **akāmadam**
anabhilaṣita-pradam \|

nanu śrīr yaṁ nityam anu bhajate, taṁ prati katham evaṁ paruṣa-bhāṣiṇyo
bhavatyaḥ ? ity āha---**śriyam ṛte** śriyaṁ vinā tad-vārtā
[dūretyatām]{.mark} ity arthaḥ \| śrīs tāvat tasya doṣaṁ na paśyati
sva-kārya-mātra-sādhikā, **saiva** striyas tāvad asmādṛśya
**eka-niṣṭhā** ekasmin premaṇy eva niṣṭhā yāsām \| ataḥ kṣīṇa-premāṇaṁ
kathaṁ kena prakāreṇa **bhajāma** ity asūyā vyabhicārī bhāvaḥ \|\|24\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (prīti-sandarbhaḥ 387**): tadaiva daivād āgataṁ haṁsaṁ
dūtaṁ kalpayitvāhuḥ---**haṁsa** iti \| **no**'smān prati **purā** rahasi
**uktaṁ kiṁ vā smarati** \| smaratu mām evety āśayenāhuḥ---**tam** iti
\| yadi ca tad-āgrahaḥ, tadā he **kṣaudra** sauhṛdya-cāñcalyena
kṣudrasya tasya dūta, tam eva **kāmadaṁ** yuvati-jana-kṣobhakam atra
**ālāpaya** āhvaya \| kintu yām āsādya vayaṁ tyaktāḥ, tāṁ **śriyam ṛte**
\| tāṁ solluṇṭhaṁ stauti \| **striyāṁ** madhye **saiva ekatra** tasmin
**niṣṭhā** yasyāḥ, tādṛśī \| tataḥ kathaṁ tasyāṁ nāsajyeta ? iti
vyañjitam \| kākvā sveṣām api tan-niṣṭhatvaṁ vyajya solluṇṭhatvaṁ
darśitam \|\|24\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kam api haṁsaṁ dūtaṁ
prakalpyāhuḥ---**haṁsa** iti \| nanu bhavatīr vinā sa kathaṁ svasty
āstām ? iti cet, **uktaṁ** **purā**\--na tvādṛśīṁ praṇayinīṁ gṛhiṇīṁ
gṛheṣu paśyāmi \[bhā.pu. 10.60.55\] ity-ādi sva-prema-vākyaṁ smarati kim
? kiṁ vā, **cala-sauhṛdaḥ** san smarati \| nanu smṛtvaiva māṁ
prasthāpitavān atas tad-antikaṁ calata \|

taṁ bhajateti tatrāhuḥ---**kasmād** iti \| sa ced asmān na bhajeta, nāpy
avagacchati, tarhi **vayaṁ kasmād bhajāmaḥ** ? kasmād vā yāmaḥ ? bhoḥ
karuṇā-sindhavaḥ ! tarhi kāma-pīḍitasya tasya kathaṁ nistāraḥ ?
tatrāhuḥ---he **kṣaudra** ! kṣudrasya dūta ! **ālāpaya** atraiva taṁ
**kāmadaṁ** kāma-pīḍitam api darśana-mātreṇaiva kāma-pīḍā-pradam ākāraya
\| sa asmān āyātu, na tu garvavatyo vayaṁ taṁ yāma iti bhāvaḥ \| om iti
gacchantaṁ taṁ matvā punar āhuḥ---yāhy asmān vañcayitvā ekākinī ramate
tāṁ **śriyam ṛte** tam eva kevalam ākāraya \|

nanu sā tad-eka-niṣṭhā kathaṁ parihartuṁ śakyā syāt ? ata
āhuḥ---**striyām** iti jātāv eka-vacanam \| strīṣv asmāsu madhye **sā
eva** kim **eka-niṣṭhā** aikāntikī, na tu vayam ity arthaḥ \|
\"kṣaudrālāpam akāmadam\" iti pāṭhe **kṣaudraṁ** madhu, tadvan
madhurālāpa-mātraṁ yasya, tam **akāmadam** arati-pradaṁ, **taṁ śriyam
ṛte vayaṁ kasmād bhajāmaḥ** ? kintv anādṛtā satī saiva punaḥ punar
bhajatu, yato'smādṛśyo māninyaḥ striyaḥ, **striyāṁ** strīṣu madhye
**eka-niṣṭhāḥ** ekatraiva sva-māna-siddhau niṣṭhā yāsāṁ tāḥ \|\|24\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.25 \|\|**

**śrī-śuka uvāca---**

**itīdṛśena bhāvena kṛṣṇe yogeśvareśvare \|**

**kriyamāṇena mādhavyo lebhire vaiṣṇavīṁ**[^13] **gatim \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : iti** ittham \| **bhāvena**
premṇā \| **mādhavyo** mādhava-bhāryāḥ \| atīva-prema-vaśa-vivaśānāṁ
kṣaṇika-viyoge'pi citta-vibhramo bhavaty eveti bhāvaḥ \|\|25\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) : itīdṛśena** ity-ādi \|
**īdṛśena** evaṁ-vidhena **bhāvena** mādhave kriyamāṇena **vaiṣṇavīṁ**
**gatiṁ** bhāgavatīṁ bhaktiṁ **lebhire**, animittā bhāgavatī bhaktiḥ
siddher garīyasī \[bhā.pu. 3.25.23\] iti \| yasyā lakṣaṇaṁ tenāsāṁ
parama-bhāgavatatvam āyātam \| tena satsv api bahuṣu upāsanā-śarīreṣu
prema-mātraika-niṣṭhāyām upāsanāyāṁ pati-bhāvena bhajana-kṣamaṁ śarīram
eva svarūpa-yogyam, tat tu śrī-kṛṣṇopāsanāyām eva tasya
paramānanda-mūrtitvāt \| tāsāṁ cānanya-sādhāraṇānurāgavattvāt,
sarvendriya-pravṛttyā tatra praveśāt \|\|25\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** itthaṁ phalitaṁ
tādṛśa-premaiva \| evaṁ śrī-bhagavad-vaśīkaraṇa-premavatīnāṁ tāsāṁ
māhātmyam āha---**iti** iti \| ataḥ kiṁ vā anenokta-prakāreṇa ya īdṛśa
ukta-sadṛśo **bhāvaḥ**, tena \| sa ca bhāvas tasyaiva māhātmyād ity
abhiprāyeṇāha---**kṛṣṇe** sarvathā sarva-cittākarṣaka iti \| anyeṣāṁ
cāsau sudurlabha ity āśayenāha---**yogeśvarāṇām** api **īśvare**,
kathañcit prayatnena manasā sevye \|

yad vā, kiṁ ca yogeti sva-śakti-viśeṣeṇa pratyekaṁ sarvāsām eva tāsāṁ
sarvathā yugapad ramaṇād ity arthaḥ \| **kriyamāṇena** sadā
vidhīyamāneneti tasmiṁs tāsām atṛptir bhāvānivṛttiś coktā \|
**madhavyo** madhu-vaṁśodbhavasya tasya patnyaḥ \| **viṣṇur**
nijāśeṣaiśvarya-prakaṭanena viśva-vyāpako bhagavān śrī-kṛṣṇa eva,
tadīyāṁ **gatiṁ** daśāṁ **lebhire**, yādṛśo'sau syāt tā api tādṛśya eva
bhaveyur ity arthaḥ \|

yad vā, **gatiṁ** parama-vilāsa-prakāraṁ priya-jana-paravaśo'yaṁ mayaiva
saha sadā bahudhā viharann āste \| na kathañcit kadācid api viyujyata
ity-ādinā lakṣaṇaṁ pratyekaṁ sākṣād anvabhavan ity arthaḥ \|\|25\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** itthaṁ bhaṇitaṁ
phalita-tādṛśa-premavatīnāṁ tāsāṁ māhātmyam āha---**iti** iti \|
anenokta-rītikena **īdṛśena** cānyenānyena **kṛṣṇe** svayaṁ bhagavati \|
ata eva yogeśvare parama-durlabhe ity arthaḥ \| kriyamāṇena sadā
vidhīyamāneneti tasmiṁs tāsām atṛptir bhāvānivṛttiś ca sūcitā \|
**madhavyo** madhu-vaṁśodbhavasya tasya patnyaḥ \| **viṣṇuḥ** svayaṁ
bhagavattvāt sarva-vyāpakaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa eva, tadīyāṁ **gatiṁ** daśāṁ
**lebhire** yādṛśa evāsau syāt, tā api tādṛśya eva bhaveyur ity arthaḥ
\|

yad vā, sa yathā sarva-vyāpakaḥ, tathā tā api tasya vyāpikā jātā ity
arthaḥ \| \"paramām\" iti pāṭhe tv aprakaṭa-rūpām alaukikīm ity arthaḥ
\| śānacaḥ prayogeṇa vyavadhānāvagatyā kāsāṁcid arjuna-parājayānantaraṁ
gaty-antaraṁ tu māyika-mātram ity abhyupagatam \| tac ca yuktaṁ
vivāha-prasaṅge tāsāṁ tat-svarūpa-śaktitvena darśitatvāt \|\|25\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** **itīdṛśena vaiṣṇavīṁ** sarvatra
paripūrṇasya śrī-kṛṣṇasya **gatiṁ lebhire** \| tatra **kriyamāṇair** api
vartamāna-prayogeṇa vyavadhānaṁ ca nirastam \| ataḥ kāsāṁcid
arjuna-parājayānantara-gaty-antaraṁ māyikam evety abhyupagatam
\|\|25\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** upasaṁharati---**iti**
ity-ādi \| evaṁ prakāreṇa bhāvena vaicittyākhyena bhāvena \| kīdṛśena ?
**kṛṣṇe kriyamāṇena** \| kṛṣṇe kīdṛśe ? **yogeśvarāṇām** api **īśvare**
\| **mādhavyo** mahiṣyaḥ \| **vaiṣṇavīṁ gatiṁ lebhire** vaiṣṇavīyāṁ
gatiṁ rukmiṇī-sādṛśyaṁ rukmiṇī yathā nitya-priyā tathaivābhavan ity
arthaḥ \| viṣṇuḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ, tat-svarūpā vaiṣṇavī tasyeyam iti vā
vaiṣṇavīha rukmiṇī vaiṣṇavīyām ity arthe vaiṣṇavīti chāndasam \| athavā
viṣṇuḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ, **vaiṣṇavīṁ** viṣṇu-devatākāṁ **gatiṁ** prema
\|\|25\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (prīti-sandarbhaḥ 388) :** atha tāsāṁ
tad-vidhāśeṣa-vipralambhānantarajaṁ nityam eva sarvātmaka-sambhogam
āha---**itīdṛśena** \| **viṣṇoḥ** śrī-kṛṣṇasya eva sambandhinīṁ
**gatiṁ** nitya-saṁyogaṁ **lebhire** \| atra hetuḥ---**mādhavyaḥ**
madhu-vaṁśodbhavasya śrī-kṛṣṇasyaiva nitya-preyasyas tāḥ \|\|25\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tāsām
etādṛśa-śrī-kṛṣṇa-viṣayaka-bhāvavatīnāṁ kiṁ prāpyaṁ vastv ity apekṣāyām
āhuḥ---**iti** iti \| **vaiṣṇavīṁ** vaiṣṇava-prāpyāṁ prema-bhaktim eva
tāsām aprākṛtīnāṁ bhagavan-nitya-preyasīnāṁ sac-cid-ānanda-vapuṣāṁ
brahma-rasāsvādādhika-bhagavan-mādhuryāsvādavatīnāṁ punar
mokṣādi-phala-prāpty-abhāva-sambhavāt premādhikyam evety arthaḥ \| yad
vā, vaiṣṇavīṁ viṣṇos tasyaiva kṛṣṇasya bhāvonmāda-prauḍhimnā
tādātmya-mayīṁ rāsāntardhāne vraja-sundaryo nānā-praśnādy-anantaram
unmādasya prauḍhimnā yathā kṛṣṇo'haṁ paśyata gatim iti
kṛṣṇa-tādātmya-mayīṁ lebhire tathaivaitā api kurary-ādi-praśnānantaraṁ
tām evety arthaḥ \| prema-vaicittyādi-kṛṣṇa-tādātmyādi-daśā
anurāga-vilāsā eva yadu-mahiṣīṇām anurāga-paryantā daśā
śrīmad-ujjvala-nīlamaṇau vyākhyātā eva \|\|25\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.26 \|\|**

**śruta-mātro'pi yaḥ strīṇāṁ prasahyākarṣate manaḥ \|**

**uru-gāyoru-gīto vā paśyantīnāṁ ca kiṁ punaḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** tāsāṁ kṛṣṇe evaṁ-bhūto bhāvo
nāticitram ity āha---**śruta-mātro'pi** iti \| **urubhir** **gāyair**
gītair urudhā gīto vā, yaiḥ kaiścid api gītaiḥ kathābhiḥ, kathañcid api
gīto vety arthaḥ \|\|26\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** *evaṁ-bhūtaś*
citta-vibhrama-karaḥ \| *bhāvaḥ* premā \| *urubhir* anantaiḥ \| urudhā
anekadhā \| *ity artha* iti---yena kenacit saṁskṛtena prākṛtena vā
*gītena* **gīto**'pi śrī-kṛṣṇaś cec ceta-ākarṣaṇaṁ karoti, tadā kim u
vaktavyaṁ **paśyatāṁ** ceta-ākarṣaṇaṁ vṛttam iti kaimutyam uktam
\|\|26\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** evaṁ strīṇām eva
tat-karaṇaka-sukhākarṣaṇavattāṁ darśayann āha---**śruta-mātro'pi**
ity-ādi \| śravaṇa-manana-nididhyāsanair nahi bhagavati mano-layo
bhavati, āsāṁ tu śravaṇa-mātreṇaiva katham etat ? tatrāha---yaḥ svayam
eva śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ **prasahya** balād balātkāreṇa tāsāṁ **mana ākarṣayati**
śravaṇa-mananādivatāṁ tu mano madīya-mānasam api kadācid vaśīkaroti na
vā, **paśyantīnāṁ** tu yan mana ākṛṣyate, tat **punaḥ kim** ? \|\|26\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) : śruta-mātro'py**
**uru-gāya** uru gāyo gīto vāpi **strīṇāṁ mana ākarṣati**\| sākṣāt
**paśyantīnāṁ** tu **mana ākarṣati** iti **kiṁ punar** vaktavyam ? ity
arthaḥ \| pāṭhāntare'pi sa evārthaḥ \| tatra śravaṇe
cittābhiniveśāpekṣayā gāne ca teṣāṁ vyākhyānusāreṇa kiñcit
sambandha-mātreṇa tasya nyūnatāpekṣayā vā-śabdaḥ \| anyat tair
vyākhyātam \|

yad vā, uru-gāyair bahu-gītair urudhā gīto vākarṣatīti kiṁ vaktavyam ?
tatrāpi kiṁ punar vaktavyam paśyantīnāṁ tv ākarṣatīty arthaḥ \| evaṁ
śravaṇāder yathottaraṁ śraiṣṭhyaṁ sidhyed eva \| atas tat-patnīnāṁ
mahā-saubhāgyavatīnāṁ sadā tena saha bahudhā viharantīnāṁ tāsāṁ tādṛśo
bhāvo yukta eveti bhāvaḥ \|\|26\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** tatra tasyāpi māhātmyam
āha---**śruta-mātro'pi yaḥ strīṇāṁ mana ākarṣati** \| **urubhir gāyair**
gītaiḥ prabandhair uru yathā syāt, tathā **gītas** tad-viṣayīkṛto vā
**kiṁ punaḥ** tatrāpi sākṣāt **paśyantīnāṁ** tu kiṁ punar vaktavyam ?
ity arthaḥ \| \"kutaḥ punaḥ\" iti pāṭhe'pi sa evārthaḥ \| atas
tat-patnīnāṁ svābhāvika-mahā-premavatīnāṁ sadā tena saha viharantīnāṁ
tāsāṁ tādṛśa eva bhāvo yuktaḥ kvacid anyathā śravaṇaṁ tu munīnām api
moha-śravaṇād eva, ity aṅgopadiśanty eke vismṛtya prāg udāhṛtam itivat
\[bhā.pu. 10.57.31\] iti bhāvaḥ \|\|26\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** nanu tāsāṁ yadīdṛk daśā
bhaviṣyati, tat kim ? ity āha---**śruta-mātro'pi** ity-ādi \| yaḥ
śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ **śruta-mātro'pi strīṇāṁ manaḥ prasahya ākarṣate**, sa eva
**paśyantīnāṁ** yad ākarṣiṣyati, tat kim ? tatrāpi yābhiḥ saha satataṁ
viharati, tāsāṁ tu yad evaṁ bhaviṣyati, tat kiṁ vaktavyam iti śeṣaḥ \|
kīdṛśaḥ ? **uru-gāyaiḥ** puṇya-ślokaiḥ uru yathā syāt tathā gītam \|
**vā** ity āścarye \|\|26\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : urubhir gāna**-prabandhair
uru yathā syāt tathā **gītaḥ** sa **paśyantīnāṁ** tu **kuta** iti śabdas
tv-arthe \|\|26\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.27 \|\|**

**yāḥ samparyacaran premṇā pāda-saṁvāhanādibhiḥ \|**

**jagad-guruṁ bhartṛ-buddhyā tāsāṁ kiṁ varṇyate tapaḥ \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** **yā** rukmiṇy-ādyāḥ \|
**kiṁ**-śabdas tapo-mahattvaṁ vakti \|\|27\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** evaṁ sāmānyataḥ
strīṇāṁ bhajane svarūpa-yogyatām uktvā viśeṣam āha---**yā** ity-ādi \|
**yāḥ** punar **bhartṛ**-bhāvena **premṇā** pāda-saṁvāhanādibhiḥ
paryacaran, **tāsāṁ** **tapaḥ kiṁ varṇyate** ? anyeṣāṁ tu bhāvāntareṇa
bhajatāṁ tapo varṇayituṁ śakyata eveti bhāvaḥ \| ataḥ sarvajña-janebhyo
bhartṛ-bhāvena bhajanam eva śreya iti rahasyam \|\|27\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** atas tā eva
parama-dhanyāḥ, na tv anye kecaneti bhāva-viśeṣodayenāha---**yā** iti \|
**samyak** tad-anyāśeṣāpekṣayā tat-tad-eka-niṣṭhatvādinā **paryacarann**
asevanta \| ādi-śabdāt **pāda**-prakṣalaṇa-keśa-prasādhana-vījanādayaḥ
\| **jagatāṁ** śrī-brahmādīnāṁ sarveṣām api **guruṁ** parama-pūjyam iti
mahā-daurlabhyam uktam \| **bhartṛ-buddhyā** patitvenety arthaḥ \|
**tapo** bhāgyaṁ **kiṁ varṇyate** ? api tu tan-māhātmyaṁ varṇayituṁ na
śakyata ity arthaḥ \| **bhartṛ-buddhyā** ity anenātmanaḥ
śrī-bādarāyaṇinā śrī-gopī-bhāvaḥ sūcita eva \| sarvathā sarvataḥ
premṇotkṛṣṭatare'pi vraja-vadhū-bhāve bhāva-viśeṣeṇātṛptyā
svacchanda-sevāpekṣayā bhartṛtvasyaiva bahu-mānād iti \| itthaṁ
śrī-mahiṣy-ādibhiḥ saha vividha-krīḍārthaṁ śrī-bhagavaty api gārhasthyam
evādṛtya tan-māhātmyaṁ darśitam iti \| kiṁ vā, aho kiṁ vaktavyam,
nija-priyatamās tās tena tathānugṛhītā iti \|\|27\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** atas tā eva dhanyāḥ, na tv
anye kecaneti bhāva-viśeṣodayenāha---**yā** iti \| **yāḥ** kāścid anyā
api **bhartṛ-buddhyā** bhāvanā-mātra-gamyenāpi bhartṛtvena na tu
sākṣād-bhartṛtvena yaḥ **premā**, tena yāni **pāda-saṁvāhanādīni**
mānasa-rūpāṇi, tair **jagad-guruṁ** parama-puruṣottamaṁ **samyak**
tad-eka-niṣṭhayā **paryacaran** asevanta ity arthaḥ \| **tāsāṁ tapas**
tad-upāsanā-bhāgyaṁ **kiṁ varṇyate**, api tu varṇayituṁ na śakyata ity
arthaḥ \| sākṣād-bhartṛtvena nityam eva tathā sevamānānāṁ tāsāṁ vārtā
dūrata eveti bhāvaḥ \|\|27\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** tad evāha---**yāḥ
samparyacarann** ity-ādi \| yā mādhavyaḥ **jagad-guruṁ** śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ
**bhartṛ-buddhyā** **samyak paryacaran,** tatrāpi **premṇā** \| nanu
kāmena **pāda-saṁvāhanādibhiḥ** kriyābhiḥ **tāsāṁ** **tapaḥ kiṁ
varṇyate** ? tad varṇanīyaṁ na bhavati \| anyasyānyad varṇayituṁ
śakyate, na tad iti bhāvaḥ \| ato ye māṁ bhajanti dāmpatye tapasā
vrata-caryayā \[bhā.pu. 10.60.52\] iti pūrvaṁ yad vyākhyātaṁ, tat sādhu
\|\|27\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : tāsāṁ kiṁ tapo varṇyate** ?
naiva varṇyate, kintu nitya-siddhā eva tā iti bhāvaḥ \| yad vā, tāsu
madhye kāsāñcit sādhana-siddhānāṁ kīdṛśaṁ prāktanaṁ tapa iti ced
atrāha---**yā** iti \|\|27\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.28 \|\|**

**evaṁ vedoditaṁ dharmam anutiṣṭhan satāṁ gatiḥ \|**

**gṛhaṁ dharmārtha-kāmānāṁ muhuś cādārśayat padam \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : padaṁ** sthānam \|\|28\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** **gṛhaṁ** gṛhastham \|
**padaṁ** sthānam \|\|28\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** dharmādi-parā api
svācāreṇa śikṣayitvā samuddhṛtā ity āśayenāha---**evam** iti \|
anenokta-prakāreṇa \| **satāṁ gatir** iti sādhuṣu kṛpayā
sad-dharma-pravartanārtham iti \| kiṁ vā, **satāṁ** dharmādi-parāṇāṁ
**gatir** gamya iti \| tais teṣām api sa eva sādhya iti \| yad vā,
sva-bhaktānām eva sukhārtham iti bhāvaḥ \| muhur ity anutiṣṭhann ity
anena **adarśayad** ity anenaiva vānvayaḥ \| tataś ca darśane
paunaḥpunyaṁ tad-dārḍhy-artham \|\|28\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** tad evaṁ tasya krīḍātvenaiva
sphuṭaṁ pratīyamānaṁ caritaṁ varṇayitvā tādṛśatvam eva vaidha-karmaṇy
apy atidiśan sarveṣām api śarmadatvam āha---**evaṁ satāṁ gatiḥ**
tat-krīḍaika-parama-bhaktānāṁ **gatiḥ** san vedoditaṁ **dharmaṁ**
yajñādikaṁ ca muhur anutiṣṭhan **gṛhaṁ** khalu **dharmārtha-kāmānāṁ
padam** ity apy **adarśayat** \| anyebhya upādiśad iti yataḥ **satāṁ**
tat-krīḍaika-jīvānāṁ dharmādi-parāṇāṁ ca **gatir** āśrayaḥ \|\|28\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ, bṛhat-krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** *na
vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : padaṁ** sthānam \|\|28\|\|

**\...**

**\|\| 10.90.29 \|\|**

**āsthitasya paraṁ dharmaṁ kṛṣṇasya gṛha-medhinām \|**

**āsan ṣoḍaśa-sāhasraṁ mahiṣyaś ca śatādhikam \|\|**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) :** **param**
atithi-pūjanādinotkṛṣṭam \|\|29\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** *na vyākhyātam.*

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**sanātana-gosvāmī (bṛhad-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** tathā
tad-gārhasthya-bhūtānāṁ śrī-bhagavat-putrādīnāṁ sarveṣāṁ yādavānām api
māhātmyam uktvānuvāda-pūrvakaṁ varṇayati---**āsthitasya** ity-ādīnāṁ
**param** utkṛṣṭaṁ prāyaḥ sarveṣām apy āśramiṇām āśrayatvāt \| tad
uktaṁ---

> bhikṣā-bhujaś ca ye kecit parivrāḍ-brahmacāriṇaḥ \|
>
> te'py atraiva pratiṣṭhante gārhasthyaṁ tena vai varam \|\| iti \|

yad vā, **paraṁ** mukhyaṁ mukhya-kalpatvena kṛtatvāt **kṛṣṇasya**
aśeṣaiśvarya-prakaṭanārtham avatīrṇasya svayaṁ bhagavataḥ \| yad vā,
tad-dharmānuṣṭhāna-mādhuryeṇāpi sarva-cittākarṣakasya \| **tu**-śabdo
bhede \| mahā-**mahiṣyas** tāvad aṣṭāv āsann eva ṣoḍaśa-sāhasraṁ
**mahiṣyas tu śatādhikaṁ** yathā syāt tathāsan \| \"mahiṣyaś ca\" iti
pāṭhe'pi sa evārthaḥ \|\|29\|\|

[\[?\]]{.mark} dharmādīnāṁ sarveṣāṁ yādavānām api māhātmyam
uktvānuvāda-pūrvakaṁ varṇayiṣyann anuṣṭhita-dharmam eva
prapañcayati---**āsthitasya** ity-ādinā, jajñire \[bhā.pu. 10.90.39\]
ity-antena \| param utkṛṣṭaṁ prāyaḥ sarveṣām apy āśramiṇām āśrayatvāt \|
tad uktaṁ---

> bhikṣā-bhujaś ca ye kecit parivrāḍ brahmacāriṇaḥ \|
>
> te'py atraiva pratiṣṭhante gārhasthyaṁ tena vai varam \|\| iti \|

yad vā, **mukhyaṁ** mukhya-kalpatvena kṛtatvāt \| kṛṣṇasya
aśeṣaiśvarya-prakaṭanārtham avatīrṇasya bhagavataḥ \| kiṁ vā,
tad-dharmānuṣṭhānena sarva-cittākarṣakasya \| **tu**-śabdaś
cārthe'nuktvā aṣṭau samuccinoti \| yad vā, suprasiddhena prāyikatvena vā
tad-anuktiḥ \| tataś ca tu-śabdo viśeṣe, anyāśeṣa-gṛhibhyo vailakṣaṇyāt
\|\|29\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**jīva-gosvāmī (laghu-vaiṣṇava-toṣaṇī) :** tathā tad-gārhasthya-bhūtānāṁ
śrī-bhagavat-putrādīnāṁ sarveṣāṁ yādavānām api māhātmyam
uktvānuvāda-pūrvakaṁ varṇayati---**āsthitasya** ity-ādīnāṁ **param**
utkṛṣṭaṁ prāyaḥ sarveṣām apy āśramiṇām āśrayatvāt \| tad uktaṁ---

> bhikṣā-bhujaś ca ye kecit parivrāḍ brahmacāriṇaḥ \|
>
> te'py atraiva pratiṣṭhante gārhasthyaṁ tena vai varam \|\| iti \|

yad vā, **paraṁ** mukhyaṁ mukhya-kalpatvena kṛtatvāt **kṛṣṇasya**
aśeṣaiśvarya-prakaṭanārtham avatīrṇasya svayaṁ bhagavataḥ \| yad vā,
tad-dharmānuṣṭhāna-mādhuryeṇāpi sarva-cittākarṣakasya \| **tu**-śabdo
bhede \| mahā-**mahiṣyas** tāvad aṣṭāv āsann eva ṣoḍaśa-sāhasraṁ
**mahiṣyas tu śatādhikaṁ** yathā syāt, tathāsan \| \"mahiṣyaś ca\" iti
pāṭhe'pi sa evārthaḥ \|\|29\|\|

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
